Private Sub CarregaCreditos()
    ' Mostra créditos que ainda não estão totalmente pagos, e os créditos a 0 que ainda não tem factura.
    Dim criterio As String
    criterio = "(cdTotal > 0 OR cdTotalDescontos > 0 OR cdTotalComp > 0) AND (xpago < cdtotal OR cdVenFacturada = 0)"
    
    ' Chave Creditos indica que só devem ser mostrados os créditos do armazém corrente
    If Not ObtemSettingBool("Creditos_MostraTodasLojas") Then
        criterio = criterio & " AND cdidarmazem = " & aUser(C_UserArmazemId)
    End If
    
    ' Lista
    Dim orderBy As String
    Select Case sOrderCreditos
        Case "Obra" 'num obra
            orderBy = "ORDER BY cdNumObra"
           
        Case "Venda" ' num venda
            orderBy = "ORDER BY cdNumVenda"
            
        Case "Doc" ' tipo de documento
            orderBy = "ORDER BY cdVenFacturada"
            
        Case "Cliente" ' Nome
            orderBy = "ORDER BY xNomeCli"
            
        Case "ReferenciaExterna"
            orderBy = "ORDER BY ReferenciaExterna"
            
        Case Else ' Data
            orderBy = "ORDER BY cdData DESC, cdId DESC"
    End Select
    
    Set datCreditos.Recordset = dbo.OpenRecordset("SELECT * FROM qyCreditos WHERE " & criterio & " " & orderBy, dbOpenDynaset)
    
    ' Botões
    ActivaBotoesPos ValoresPagamento, (datCreditos.Recordset.RecordCount > 0)
    With datCreditos.Recordset
        If (.RecordCount > 0) Then
            timObservacoes.Enabled = (!cliObservacoes & vbNullString <> vbNullString)
        End If
    End With
    
    ' Totais
    Dim rsTotais As Recordset
    Set rsTotais = dbo.OpenRecordset("SELECT SUM(xPago) AS TotPago, SUM(cdDivida) AS TotDivida FROM qyCreditos WHERE " & criterio, dbOpenForwardOnly)
    With rsTotais
        If Not .EOF Then
            lblTxtPendente(0).Caption = Format(!TotPago, "Standard")
            lblTxtPendente(0).ToolTipText = ConvertMoeda(!TotPago)
            
            lblTxtPendente(1).Caption = Format(!TotDivida, "Standard")
            lblTxtPendente(1).ToolTipText = ConvertMoeda(!TotDivida)
        End If
        .Close
    End With
    
    tdgCreditos.Columns(18).Visible = ObtemSettingBool("Creditos_ReferenciaExterna")
    tdgCreditos.Columns(18).Order = 6
    tdgCreditos.Columns(18).Width = 1500
End Sub

Private Sub DocumentoClienteEditar(ByVal Operacao As Integer)
    On Error GoTo erro
    
    Dim docID As Long
    docID = datDoc.Recordset!cabDocID
    
    If UsaDocumentosDotNet Then
        OptiwareEx.DocumentoVendaConsulta docID
    Else
        Dim oHeader As clsDocClienteHeader
        Set oHeader = New clsDocClienteHeader
        oHeader.Carrega datDoc.Recordset!cabDocID

        'Mostra o Form do Documento
        With frmPOSDocumento
            Set .Cabecalho = oHeader
            .Operacao = Operacao
            .Show vbModal
        End With
        Unload frmPOSDocumento
    End If
    
    DocumentoClienteUpdateList docID
    Exit Sub
erro:
    ErrorHandle "frmPosMain", "DocumentoClienteEditar()", Operacao
End Sub

Private Function DocumentoClienteUpdateList(Optional ByVal DocumentoID As Long = 0) As Boolean

    Dim iErro As Integer

    On Error GoTo erro

    DocumentoClienteUpdateList = False

    With datDoc.Recordset
        RsRequery datDoc.Recordset
        
        If (DocumentoID > 0) Then
            If (.RecordCount > 0) Then
                .FindFirst "cabdocID = " & DocumentoID
                If .NoMatch Then
                    .MoveFirst
                End If
            End If
        End If
    End With

    DocumentoClienteUpdateList = True

    Exit Function

erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "DocumentoClienteUpdateList()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:
    bSemaforo bClose
End Function
Private Function GravarLC(ByVal FornecedorReferencia As String, _
                          ByVal TipoReferencia As String, _
                          ByVal ComposicaoReferencia As String, _
                          ByVal ColoracaoReferencia As String, _
                          ByVal LenteReferencia As String, _
                          ByVal LenteDesignacao As String, _
                          ByVal LenteApresentacao As String, _
                          ByVal LentePrecoVenda As Double, _
                          ByVal LentePrecoCusto As Double, _
                          ByVal LenteIva As Double, _
                          ByRef LenteID As Long, _
                          ByRef IvaID As Long, _
                          ByRef FamiliaID As Long, _
                          ByRef Referencia As String) As Integer

    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim fCreate As Boolean
    Dim iResult As Integer
    Dim lID As Long
    Dim Tabela As Recordset, rsFamilias As Recordset, rsIva As Recordset

    On Error GoTo erro

    Set Tabela = dbo.OpenRecordset("LC", dbOpenTable)
    Set rsFamilias = dbo.OpenRecordset("Familias", dbOpenTable)
    Set rsIva = dbo.OpenRecordset("Iva", dbOpenTable)

    With rsFamilias
        If (.RecordCount > 0) Then
            .Index = "famNome"
            .Seek "=", "Lentes de Contacto"
            If Not .NoMatch Then
                FamiliaID = !famID
            End If
        End If
        .Close
    End With

    fCreate = False
    With rsIva
        If (.RecordCount > 0) Then
            .Index = "ivaAno"
            .Seek "=", Year(Date), LenteIva
            If .NoMatch Then
                fCreate = True
            End If
        Else
            fCreate = True
        End If

        If fCreate Then
            .AddNew
            !ivaCreator = aUser(C_UserLogin)
            !ivaModified = Now
            !ivaAno = Year(Date)
            !IvaPercentagem = LenteIva
            RsUpdate rsIva
            .bookmark = .LastModified
        End If
        IvaID = !IvaID
        .Close
    End With

    If (ColoracaoReferencia = vbNullString) Then ColoracaoReferencia = "0000"
    Referencia = "0000" & LenteReferencia & ColoracaoReferencia
    Referencia = Referencia & oUtils.CheckDigit(Referencia)

    fCreate = False
    With Tabela
        If (.RecordCount > 0) Then
            .FindFirst _
                "lcRefLente = " & SqlStr(LenteReferencia) & _
                " AND lcRefColoracao = " & SqlStr(ColoracaoReferencia)
                
            .Index = "lcReferencia"
            .Seek "=", Referencia
            If .NoMatch Then
                fCreate = True
            End If
        Else
            fCreate = True
        End If

        If fCreate Then
            .AddNew
            !lcCreator = aUser(C_UserLogin)
            !lcModified = Now
            !lcRefFornecedor = FornecedorReferencia
            !lcRefTipoLente = TipoReferencia
            !lcRefComposicao = ComposicaoReferencia
            !lcRefColoracao = ColoracaoReferencia
            !lcRefLente = LenteReferencia
            !lcDesignacao = LenteDesignacao
            !lcApresentacao = LenteApresentacao
            !lcPrecoVenda = LentePrecoVenda
            !lcPrecoCusto = LentePrecoCusto
            !lcTaxaIVAID = IvaID
            !lcReferencia = Referencia
            !lcFamiliaID = FamiliaID
            !lcMoeda = aEuro(C_TipoMoeda)    'FMD
            !lcTaxaCV = aEuro(C_TaxaEuro)    'FMD
            RsUpdate Tabela
            .bookmark = .LastModified
        End If
        LenteID = !lcid
        .Close
    End With

    iResult = RES_SUCCESS

    GoTo Fim

    Exit Function

erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "GravarLC()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    iResult = RES_FAILURE
Fim:
    Set Tabela = Nothing
    Set rsFamilias = Nothing
    Set rsIva = Nothing
    GravarLC = iResult
End Function
Private Function GravarLCColoracao(ByVal Referencia As String, ByVal Designacao As String) As Integer

    Dim fCreate As Boolean
    Dim iResult As Integer
    Dim Tabela As Recordset
    Dim iErro As Integer

    On Error GoTo erro

    Set Tabela = dbo.OpenRecordset("LCColoracao", dbOpenTable)

    If (Referencia <> vbNullString) Then
        With Tabela
            If (.RecordCount > 0) Then
                .Index = "lcclReferencia"
                .Seek "=", Referencia
                If .NoMatch Then
                    fCreate = True
                End If
            Else
                fCreate = True
            End If

            If fCreate Then
                .AddNew
                !lcclCreator = aUser(C_UserLogin)
                !lcclModified = Now
                !lcclDesignacao = Designacao
                !lcclReferencia = Referencia
                RsUpdate Tabela
            End If
            .Close
        End With
    End If

    iResult = RES_SUCCESS

    GoTo Fim

    Exit Function

erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "GravarLCColoracao()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    iResult = RES_FAILURE
Fim:
    Set Tabela = Nothing
    GravarLCColoracao = iResult
End Function

Private Function GravarLCExistencias(ByVal PrecoVenda As Double, _
                                     ByVal PrecoCusto As Double, _
                                     ByVal TaxaIVA As Double, _
                                     ByVal LenteID As Long, _
                                     ByVal IvaID As Long, _
                                     ByVal ArmazemID As Long, _
                                     ByRef ExistenciaID As Long) As Integer

    Dim fCreate As Boolean
    Dim iResult As Integer
    Dim dPrecoVenda As Double
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim Tabela As Recordset

    On Error GoTo erro

    Set Tabela = dbo.OpenRecordset("Existencias", dbOpenTable)

    dPrecoVenda = PrecoVenda / (1 + TaxaIVA / 100)
    iResult = ArredondarValor(dPrecoVenda, ARR_NENHUM, 3)
    If (iResult <> RES_SUCCESS) Then GoTo Abortar

    With Tabela
        If (.RecordCount > 0) Then
            .Index = "LCArmazemID"
            .Seek "=", LenteID, ArmazemID
            If .NoMatch Then
                fCreate = True
            End If
        Else
            fCreate = True
        End If

        If fCreate Then
            .AddNew
            !extCreator = aUser(C_UserLogin)
            !extModified = Now
            !extIDLenteContacto = LenteID
            !extIDArmazem = ArmazemID
            !extIDIVA = IvaID
            !extPrecoCusto = PrecoCusto
            !extPrecoVendaSemIva = dPrecoVenda
            !extPrecoVendaComIVA = PrecoVenda
            
            RsUpdate Tabela
            .bookmark = .LastModified
        End If
        ExistenciaID = !extID
        .Close
    End With

    iResult = RES_SUCCESS

    GoTo Fim

    Exit Function
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "GravarLCExistencias()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    iResult = RES_FAILURE
Fim:
    Set Tabela = Nothing
End Function
Private Function GravarLCFornecedores(ByVal Referencia As String, ByVal Designacao As String) As Integer

    Dim fCreate As Boolean
    Dim iResult As Integer
    Dim lID As Long
    Dim Tabela As Recordset, rsFornecedores As Recordset
    Dim iErro As Integer

    On Error GoTo erro

    Set Tabela = dbo.OpenRecordset("LCFornecedores", dbOpenTable)
    Set rsFornecedores = dbo.OpenRecordset("qyFornecedoresActivos", dbOpenSnapshot)

    With Tabela
        If (.RecordCount > 0) Then
            .Index = "lcfReferencia"
            .Seek "=", Referencia
            If .NoMatch Then
                fCreate = True
            End If
        Else
            fCreate = True
        End If

        If fCreate Then
            oDefinitions.Tabela = rsFornecedores
            oDefinitions.DefaultValues = Designacao
            oDefinitions.Action MarcaFornecedor
            If oDefinitions.Cancelar Then GoTo Fim
            lID = oDefinitions.ReturnValues

            .AddNew
            !lcfCreator = aUser(C_UserLogin)
            !lcfModified = Now
            !lcfDesignacao = Designacao
            !lcfReferencia = Referencia
            !lcfIdFichaFornecedor = lID
            RsUpdate Tabela
        End If
        .Close
    End With

    rsFornecedores.Close

    iResult = RES_SUCCESS

    GoTo Fim

    Exit Function
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "GravarLCFornecedores()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    iResult = RES_FAILURE
Fim:
    Set Tabela = Nothing
    Set rsFornecedores = Nothing
    GravarLCFornecedores = iResult
End Function
