        .Paragraph = aLoja(C_NomeLoja) & " / " & datCaixa.Recordset!cxNome & " / " & datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlcxDataAbertura
        .FontBold = False
        .CurrentY = PosicaoY(.CurrentY + 100)
        .FontSize = 8
        .MarginLeft = 100
        .MarginRight = 100
        sTableFormat = "^+4000|^+6550"
        sTableHeader = "Valores de Caixa|Valores a Inserir"
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        sTableHeader = "Entradas|Entradas"
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        f = "2000|>+2000|2550|>+2000|>+2000"
        '        s = ";{\b Numerario         }|{" & lblCxValores(1).Caption & "}|{\b Numerario                  }|{ " & txtCxDiaria(1).Text & "}|{" & lblCxValores(11).Caption & "}" & _
                 '            ";{\b Cheques           }|{" & lblCxValores(2).Caption & "}|{\b Cheques                    }|{ " & txtCxDiaria(2).Text & "}|{" & lblCxValores(12).Caption & "}" & _
                 '            ";{\b Pré-Datados       }|{" & lblCxValores(3).Caption & "}|{\b Pré-Datados                }|{ " & txtCxDiaria(3).Text & "}|{" & lblCxValores(13).Caption & "}" & _
                 '            ";{\b Multibanco        }|{" & lblCxValores(4).Caption & "}|{\b Multibanco                 }|{ " & txtCxDiaria(4).Text & "}|{" & lblCxValores(14).Caption & "}" & _
                 '            ";{\b Cartões de Credito}|{" & lblCxValores(5).Caption & "}|{\b Cartões de Crédito         }|{ " & txtCxDiaria(5).Text & "}|{" & lblCxValores(15).Caption & "}" & _
                 '            ";{\b Pag.Notas Crédito }|{" & lblCxValores(6).Caption & "}|{\b Pag.Notas Crédito          }|{ " & txtCxDiaria(6).Text & "}|{" & lblCxValores(16).Caption & "}" & _
                 '            ";{\b Pag. Vales Caixa  }|{" & lblCxValores(23).Caption & "}"
        s = "Numerário|" & lblCxValores(1).Caption & _
            "|Numerário|" & txtCxDiaria(1).Text & "|" & lblCxValores(11).Caption & ";" & _
            "Cheques|" & lblCxValores(2).Caption & _
            "|Cheques|" & txtCxDiaria(2).Text & "|" & lblCxValores(12).Caption & ";" & _
            "Pré-Datados|" & lblCxValores(3).Caption & _
            "|Pré-Datados|" & txtCxDiaria(3).Text & "|" & lblCxValores(13).Caption & ";" & _
            "Multibanco|" & lblCxValores(4).Caption & _
            "|Multibanco|" & txtCxDiaria(4).Text & "|" & lblCxValores(14).Caption & ";" & _
            "Cartões de Crédito|" & lblCxValores(5).Caption & _
            "|Cartões de Crédito|" & txtCxDiaria(5).Text & "|" & lblCxValores(15).Caption & ";" & _
            "Pag. Notas Crédito|" & lblCxValores(6).Caption & _
            "|Pag. Notas Crédito|" & txtCxDiaria(6).Text & "|" & lblCxValores(16).Caption & ";" & _
            "Pag. Transferências|" & lblCxValores(24).Caption & _
            "|Pag. Transferências|" & lblCxValores(25).Caption & "|" & Space(13) & ";" & _
            "Pag. Vales Caixa|" & lblCxValores(23).Caption
        .AddTable "<+2000|>+2000|<+2550|>+2000|>+2000", vbNullString, s

        sTableHeader = "Saídas|Saídas"
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        s = "Vales de Caixa|" & lblCxValores(7).Caption & "|Vales de Caixa|" & txtCxDiaria(7).Text & "|" & lblCxValores(17).Caption & ";" & _
            "Pagamentos|" & lblCxValores(8).Caption & "|Pagamentos|" & txtCxDiaria(8).Text & "|" & lblCxValores(18).Caption & ";" & _
            "Notas de Crédito|" & lblCxValores(9).Caption & "|Notas de Crédito|" & txtCxDiaria(9).Text & "|" & lblCxValores(19).Caption & ";" & _
            "|||;" & _
            "Total em Caixa|" & lblCxValores(10).Caption & "|Total de Contagem / Diferença|" & lblCxValores(21).Caption & "|" & lblCxValores(20).Caption & ";" & _
            "Nº Vendas do Dia|" & lblCxValores(0).Caption & ";" & _
            "Valores de Abertura|" & lblCxValores(22).Caption
        .AddTable "<+2000|>+2000|<+2550|>+2000|>+2000", vbNullString, s
        .EndDoc
    End With

    frmPrintPreview.Show vbModal

    GoTo Fim

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ImpCaixaDia()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Fim:
    Unload frmPrintPreview
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    vspImpressao.KillDoc
End Sub

' Impressao do Resumo de Caixas
Private Sub ImpCaixaResumo()
    Dim iErro As Integer
    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim sTableFormat As String, sTableHeader As String
    Dim sRecord As String, sTitulo As String
    Dim rsImpressao As Recordset
    Dim vspImpressao As vsPrinter
    Dim aValor(0 To 7) As Double
    Dim sNomeListagem As String
    With frmPrintPreview
        .impressora = ImpressoraListagens
    End With
    Set vspImpressao = frmPrintPreview.vspPreview
    Select Case cboCaixa(0).ListIndex
        Case 0    ' Todas
            sTitulo = " de todas as caixas"
        Case 1    ' Abertas
            sTitulo = " das caixas abertas"
        Case 2    ' Fechadas
            sTitulo = " das caixas fechadas"
    End Select
    If chkCaixa(0).value = 1 Then sTitulo = sTitulo & " no periodo de " & lblCaixa(2).Caption

    sNomeListagem = "Listagem de Resumo " & sTitulo

    With vspImpressao
        .PageBorder = pbBottom
        .FontName = "Arial"
        .FontSize = 7
        .FontBold = False
        .FontItalic = False
        .HdrFontName = "Arial"
        .HdrFontSize = 7
        .HdrFontBold = False
        .HdrFontItalic = False
        .Footer = sNomeListagem & "|" & Now & "| Página %d"
        .MarginTop = 600
        .MarginBottom = 650
        .MarginLeft = 600
        .MarginRight = 600
        .TextAlign = taLeftBaseline
        .TextAngle = 0
        .CurrentX = 300
        .Preview = True
    End With

    With vspImpressao
        .Orientation = orLandscape
        .StartDoc
        
        ImpressaoDoCabecalho vspImpressao, ImpressoraListagens

        Set rsImpressao = datCaixa.Recordset.Clone

        .FontSize = 10
        .FontBold = True
        .MarginLeft = 5000
        .Measure = sNomeListagem
        .CurrentY = 2750 - .TextHei
        .CurrentX = 5000
        .Text = sNomeListagem
        .FontBold = False

        .CurrentY = PosicaoY(.CurrentY + 400)
        .MarginLeft = 100
        .MarginRight = 100
        .FontSize = 7
        sTableFormat = "^+847|^+847|^+1400|^+1130|^+1130|^+1130|^+1130|^+1130|^+1130|^+1130|^+2130|^+2130"
        sTableHeader = "Data|Caixa|Estado|Valor|IVA|Descontos|Comp.|Recebimentos|Devoluções|Valor Abertura|Op.de Abertura|Op.de Fecho"

        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        sTableFormat = "^+847|<+847|^+1400|>+1130|>+1130|>+1130|>+1130|>+1130|>+1130|>+1130|<+2130|<+2130"
        rsImpressao.MoveFirst
        Do While Not rsImpressao.EOF
            sRecord = rsImpressao!ctrlcxDataAbertura & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!cxNome & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!xEstado & "|" & _
                      Format$(rsImpressao!ctrlcxTotalVendas, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format$(rsImpressao!ctrlcxTotalIva, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format$(rsImpressao!ctrlcxTotalDescontos, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format$(rsImpressao!ctrlcxTotalcomp, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format$(rsImpressao!ctrlcxTotalReceber, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format$(rsImpressao!ctrlcxTotalDevolucoes, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format$(rsImpressao!ctrlcxValorAbertura, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!xUsrAberto & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!xUsrFecho
            aValor(CxResumoValor) = rsImpressao!ctrlcxTotalVendas + aValor(CxResumoValor)
            aValor(CxResumoValorIva) = rsImpressao!ctrlcxTotalIva + aValor(CxResumoValorIva)
            aValor(CxResumoValorDesc) = rsImpressao!ctrlcxTotalDescontos + aValor(CxResumoValorDesc)
            aValor(CxResumoValorComp) = rsImpressao!ctrlcxTotalcomp + aValor(CxResumoValorComp)
            aValor(CxResumoValorRec) = rsImpressao!ctrlcxTotalReceber + aValor(CxResumoValorRec)
            aValor(CxResumoValorDev) = rsImpressao!ctrlcxTotalDevolucoes + aValor(CxResumoValorDev)
            aValor(CxResumoValorAbertura) = rsImpressao!ctrlcxValorAbertura + aValor(CxResumoValorAbertura)
            .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True
            rsImpressao.MoveNext
        Loop
        .FontBold = True

        sTableHeader = "||Totais" & MoedaListagem(True) & "|" & Format$(aValor(CxResumoValor), "Standard") & "|" & _
                       Format$(aValor(CxResumoValorIva), "Standard") & "|" & _
                       Format$(aValor(CxResumoValorDesc), "Standard") & "|" & _
                       Format$(aValor(CxResumoValorComp), "Standard") & "|" & _
                       Format$(aValor(CxResumoValorRec), "Standard") & "|" & _
                       Format$(aValor(CxResumoValorDev), "Standard") & "|" & _
                       Format$(aValor(CxResumoValorAbertura), "Standard")
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        sTableHeader = "||Totais" & MoedaListagem(False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aValor(CxResumoValor), , , False) & "|" & _
                       ConvertMoeda(aValor(CxResumoValorIva), , , False) & "|" & _
                       ConvertMoeda(aValor(CxResumoValorDesc), , , False) & "|" & _
                       ConvertMoeda(aValor(CxResumoValorComp), , , False) & "|" & _
                       ConvertMoeda(aValor(CxResumoValorRec), , , False) & "|" & _
                       ConvertMoeda(aValor(CxResumoValorDev), , , False) & "|" & _
                       ConvertMoeda(aValor(CxResumoValorAbertura), , , False)

        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        .EndDoc
    End With

    frmPrintPreview.Show vbModal

    GoTo Fim

    Exit Sub

erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ImpCaixaResumo()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Fim:
    Unload frmPrintPreview
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    vspImpressao.KillDoc
End Sub

' Impressao das Vendas do dia escolhido
Private Sub ImprimirCxVendas()
    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sTableFormat As String, sTableHeader As String
    Dim sRecord As String, strData As String, sOperador As String, sTitulo As String
    Dim vspImpressao As vsPrinter
    Dim rsImpressao As Recordset
    Dim bFirst As Boolean
    Dim iRR As Integer
    Dim aTotaisOperador(0 To 4) As Double
    Dim aTotalGeral(0 To 4) As Double
    Dim sNomeListagem As String

    With frmPrintPreview
        .impressora = ImpressoraListagens
    End With
    Set vspImpressao = frmPrintPreview.vspPreview
    bFirst = True
    sTitulo = datCaixa.Recordset!cxNome
    strData = datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlcxDataAbertura
    Set rsImpressao = datCaixaVenda.Recordset.Clone

    For iRR = 0 To 4
        aTotaisOperador(iRR) = 0
    Next iRR
    For iRR = 0 To 4
        aTotalGeral(iRR) = 0
    Next iRR

    sNomeListagem = "Listagem de Vendas da Caixa:" & sTitulo & ", Referente à Data de " & strData
    With vspImpressao
        .PageBorder = pbBottom
        .FontName = "Arial"
        .FontSize = 7
        .FontBold = False
        .FontItalic = False
        .HdrFontName = "Arial"
        .HdrFontSize = 7
        .HdrFontBold = False
        .HdrFontItalic = False
        .Footer = sNomeListagem & "| Página %d"
        .MarginTop = 600
        .MarginBottom = 650
        .MarginLeft = 600
        .MarginRight = 600
        .TextAlign = taLeftBaseline
        .TextAngle = 0
        .CurrentX = 300
        .Preview = True
    End With
    With vspImpressao
        .Orientation = orLandscape
        .StartDoc
        
        ImpressaoDoCabecalho vspImpressao, ImpressoraListagens
        
        .FontSize = 10
        .FontBold = True
        .MarginLeft = 5000
        .Measure = sNomeListagem
        .CurrentY = 2750 - .TextHei
        .CurrentX = 5000
        .Text = sNomeListagem
        .FontBold = False
        .CurrentY = PosicaoY(.CurrentY + 400)
        .MarginLeft = 100
        .MarginRight = 100
        .FontSize = 7
        sTableFormat = "^+1985|^+850|^+850|^+1400|^+1200|^+1200|^+1200|^+1200|^+2400|^+1000"
        sTableHeader = "Operador|Numero|Num. Cliente|Data|Total|Valor|Total Desconto|Total IVA|Total Comparticipação|Armazem"

        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        sTableFormat = "^+1985|^+850|^+850|^+1400|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+2400|^+1000"
        rsImpressao.MoveFirst
        sOperador = "" & rsImpressao!usrNome
        Do While Not rsImpressao.EOF
            If sOperador <> rsImpressao!usrNome Then
                sTableFormat = "^+1985|^+850|^+850|^+1400|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+2400|^+1000"
                .FontBold = True
                sRecord = "|||Total Operador|" & Format(aTotaisOperador(0), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotaisOperador(1), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotaisOperador(2), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotaisOperador(3), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotaisOperador(4), "###,###,##0.00")
                .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True
                .FontBold = False
                sOperador = rsImpressao!usrNome
                For iRR = 0 To 4
                    aTotaisOperador(iRR) = 0
                Next iRR
                bFirst = True
            Else
                sRecord = IIf(bFirst, sOperador, "") & "|" & _
                          rsImpressao!cabvenNumVenda & "|" & _
                          rsImpressao!cabposNumero & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!cabvenData, "dd-mm-yyyy") & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!xPagar, "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!CabVenTotal, "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!CabVenTotDescontos, "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!cabVenTotIva, "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!cabVenTotComp, "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!ArmNome, "###,###,##0.00")
                bFirst = False

                aTotalGeral(0) = rsImpressao!xPagar + aTotalGeral(0): aTotalGeral(1) = rsImpressao!CabVenTotal + aTotalGeral(1)
                aTotalGeral(2) = rsImpressao!CabVenTotDescontos + aTotalGeral(2): aTotalGeral(3) = rsImpressao!cabVenTotIva + aTotalGeral(3)
                aTotalGeral(4) = rsImpressao!cabVenTotComp + aTotalGeral(4)

                aTotaisOperador(0) = rsImpressao!xPagar + aTotaisOperador(0): aTotaisOperador(1) = rsImpressao!CabVenTotal + aTotaisOperador(1)
                aTotaisOperador(2) = rsImpressao!CabVenTotDescontos + aTotaisOperador(2): aTotaisOperador(3) = rsImpressao!cabVenTotIva + aTotaisOperador(3)
                aTotaisOperador(4) = rsImpressao!cabVenTotComp + aTotaisOperador(4)

                .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True
                rsImpressao.MoveNext

            End If

        Loop
        sTableFormat = "^+1985|^+850|^+850|^+1400|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+2400|^+1000"
        .FontBold = True
        sRecord = "|||Total Operador|" & Format(aTotaisOperador(0), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotaisOperador(1), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotaisOperador(2), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotaisOperador(3), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotaisOperador(4), "###,###,##0.00")
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True
        If strData >= dDataConv() Then
            sTableFormat = "^+1985|^+850|^+850|^+1400|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+2400|^+1000"
            sTableHeader = "|||Totais " & MoedaListagem(True) & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(0), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(1), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(2), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(3), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(4), "###,###,##0.00")
            .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

            sTableFormat = "^+1985|^+850|^+850|^+1400|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+2400|^+1000"
            sTableHeader = "|||Totais " & MoedaListagem(False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(0), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(1), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(2), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(3), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(4), , , False)
            .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        Else
            sTableFormat = "^+1985|^+850|^+850|^+1400|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+2400|^+1000"
            sTableHeader = "|||Totais " & MoedaListagem(False) & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(0), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(1), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(2), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(3), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(4), "###,###,##0.00")
            .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

            sTableFormat = "^+1985|^+850|^+850|^+1400|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+2400|^+1000"
            sTableHeader = "|||Totais " & MoedaListagem(True) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(0), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(1), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(2), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(3), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(4), , , False)
            .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        End If

        .EndDoc
    End With

    frmPrintPreview.Show vbModal
    Set rsImpressao = Nothing
    datCaixaVenda.Recordset.MoveFirst
    GoTo Fim

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ImprimirCxVendas()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Fim:
    Unload frmPrintPreview
Abortar:      On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    vspImpressao.KillDoc
End Sub

' Impressao do Resumo de Apuros
Private Sub ImpApurosResumo()
    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sTableFormat As String, sTableHeader As String
    Dim sTitulo As String, sRecord As String
    Dim dTotalQt As Integer, dTotalValor As Double, dTotalDesc As Double
    Dim dTotalComp As Double, dTotalRec As Double, dTotalIVA As Double
    Dim dTotalFamilia As Integer

    Dim dTotalValorEUR As Double, dTotalDescEUR As Double
    Dim dTotalCompEUR As Double, dTotalRecEUR As Double, dTotalIvaEUR As Double

    Dim vspImpressao As vsPrinter
    Dim rsImpressao As Recordset


    With frmPrintPreview
        .impressora = ImpressoraListagens
    End With
    Set vspImpressao = frmPrintPreview.vspPreview

    Set rsImpressao = datApuroGeral.Recordset.Clone

    sTitulo = "Listagem de Resumo de Apuros de Caixa"
    If chkApuroGeral(1).value = 1 Then
        Select Case cboApuroGeral(0).ListIndex
            Case 1
                sTitulo = sTitulo & " das Vendas com Documentos"
            Case 2
                sTitulo = sTitulo & " das Vendas com Talão"
            Case 3
                sTitulo = sTitulo & " de Documentos"
        End Select
    End If
    If chkApuroGeral(0).value = 1 Then
        sTitulo = sTitulo & " no intervalo de " & lblApuroGeral(1).Caption
    End If

    With vspImpressao
        .PageBorder = pbBottom
        .FontName = "Arial"
        .FontSize = 8
        .FontBold = False
        .FontItalic = False
        .HdrFontName = "Arial"
        .HdrFontSize = 8
        .HdrFontBold = False
        .HdrFontItalic = False
        .Footer = sTitulo & "| Página %d"
        .MarginTop = 600
        .MarginBottom = 650
        .MarginLeft = 600
        .MarginRight = 600
        .TextAlign = taLeftBaseline
        .TextAngle = 0
        .CurrentX = 300
        .Preview = True
    End With
    With vspImpressao
        .Orientation = orLandscape
        .StartDoc
        
        ImpressaoDoCabecalho vspImpressao, ImpressoraListagens

        .FontSize = 10
        .FontBold = True
        .MarginLeft = 5000
        .Measure = sTitulo
        .CurrentY = 2750 - .TextHei
        .CurrentX = 5000
        .Text = sTitulo
        .FontBold = False

        .CurrentY = PosicaoY(.CurrentY + 400)
        .MarginLeft = 100
        .MarginRight = 100
        .FontSize = 7
        sTableFormat = "^+1000|^+1500|^+1000|^+1400|^+1000|^+1000|^+1500|^+1500|^+1500|^+1500|^+1500"
        sTableHeader = "Caixa|Tipo Apuro|Data Inicio|Data Fim|NºFamilias|Total Qt.|Total Valor|Total Desconto|Total Comp.|Total Recebido|Total IVA"

        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        sTableFormat = "<+1000|<+1500|^+1000|^+1400|^+1000|^+1000|>+1500|>+1500|>+1500|>+1500|>+1500"
        rsImpressao.MoveFirst

        Do While Not rsImpressao.EOF
            sRecord = rsImpressao!xCaixa & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!xTipo & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!cabapDataInicio & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!cabapdatafim & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!cabapNFamilias & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!cabapTotalQt & "|" & _
                      Format(rsImpressao!cabapTotalValor, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(rsImpressao!cabapTotalDesc, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(rsImpressao!cabapTotalComp, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(rsImpressao!cabapTotalRecebido, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(rsImpressao!cabapTotalIva, "Standard") & "|"

            .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True

            dTotalFamilia = oUtils.Convert2Long(rsImpressao!cabapNFamilias) + dTotalFamilia
            dTotalQt = oUtils.Convert2Long(rsImpressao!cabapTotalQt) + dTotalQt

            If rsImpressao!cabapdatafim < dDataConv() Then
                dTotalValor = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!cabapTotalValor) + dTotalValor
                dTotalDesc = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!cabapTotalDesc) + dTotalDesc
                dTotalComp = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!cabapTotalComp) + dTotalComp
                dTotalRec = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!cabapTotalRecebido) + dTotalRec
                dTotalIVA = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!cabapTotalIva) + dTotalIVA
            Else
                dTotalValorEUR = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!cabapTotalValor) + dTotalValorEUR
                dTotalDescEUR = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!cabapTotalDesc) + dTotalDescEUR
                dTotalCompEUR = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!cabapTotalComp) + dTotalCompEUR
                dTotalRecEUR = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!cabapTotalRecebido) + dTotalRecEUR
                dTotalIvaEUR = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!cabapTotalIva) + dTotalIvaEUR
            End If
            rsImpressao.MoveNext
        Loop
        .FontBold = True
        sTableFormat = "^+1000|^+1500|^+1000|^+1400|^+1000|^+1000|>+1500|>+1500|>+1500|>+1500|>+1500"
        sTableHeader = "|||Totais EUR" & "|" & dTotalFamilia & "|" & dTotalQt & "|" & Format(dTotalValorEUR, "Standard") & "|" & Format(dTotalDescEUR, "Standard") & "|" & Format(dTotalCompEUR, "Standard") & "|" & Format(dTotalRecEUR, "Standard") & "|" & Format(dTotalIvaEUR, "Standard")
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        sTableHeader = "|||Totais ESC" & "|" & dTotalFamilia & "|" & dTotalQt & "|" & Format(dTotalValor, "Standard") & "|" & Format(dTotalDesc, "Standard") & "|" & Format(dTotalComp, "Standard") & "|" & Format(dTotalRec, "Standard") & "|" & Format(dTotalIVA, "Standard")
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        .EndDoc
    End With

    frmPrintPreview.Show vbModal
    Set rsImpressao = Nothing
    GoTo Fim

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ImpApurosResumo()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Fim:
    Unload frmPrintPreview
Abortar:      On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    vspImpressao.KillDoc
End Sub

' impressao de um apuro de uma caixa
Private Sub ImpApuroCx()
    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sTableFormat As String, sTableHeader As String
    Dim sTitulo As String, sRecord As String
    Dim vspImpressao As vsPrinter
    Dim iLinhas As Integer, iUltimo As Integer
    With frmPrintPreview
        .impressora = ImpressoraListagens
    End With
    Set vspImpressao = frmPrintPreview.vspPreview
    sTitulo = "Listagem de Apuro de Caixa"
    Select Case cboApurosCX(0).ListIndex
        Case 0
            sTitulo = sTitulo & " de Todas as Vendas"
        Case 1
            sTitulo = sTitulo & " das Vendas com Documento"
        Case 2
            sTitulo = sTitulo & " das Vendas com Talão"
        Case 3
            sTitulo = sTitulo & " de Documentos"
    End Select
    If cboApurosCX(1).ListIndex = 0 Then
        sTitulo = sTitulo & " para todas as Caixas"
    Else
        sTitulo = sTitulo & " para a " & cboApurosCX(1).Text
    End If
    sTitulo = sTitulo & " no intervalo de " & lblApurosCX(2).Caption
    With vspImpressao
        .PageBorder = pbBottom
        .FontName = "Arial"
        .FontSize = 8
        .FontBold = False
        .FontItalic = False
        .HdrFontName = "Arial"
        .HdrFontSize = 8
        .HdrFontBold = False
        .HdrFontItalic = False
        .Footer = sTitulo & "|| Página %d"
        .MarginTop = 600
        .MarginBottom = 650
        .MarginLeft = 600
        .MarginRight = 600
        .TextAlign = taLeftBaseline
        .TextAngle = 0
        .CurrentX = 300
        .Preview = True
    End With
    With vspImpressao
        .Orientation = orPortrait
        .StartDoc
        
        ImpressaoDoCabecalho vspImpressao, ImpressoraListagens
        
        .FontSize = 10
        .FontBold = True
        .MarginLeft = 5000
        .Measure = sTitulo
        .CurrentY = 2750 - .TextHei
        .CurrentX = 5000
        .Text = sTitulo
        .FontBold = False
        .CurrentY = PosicaoY(.CurrentY + 400)
        .MarginLeft = 100
        .MarginRight = 100
        .FontSize = 8
        sTableFormat = "^+2500|^+567|^+1200|^+1200|^+1200|^+1200|^+1200|^+1200"
        sTableHeader = "Familia|Qt.|Valor|Desconto|Comp.|Total|Valor de IVA|Peso"

        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        sTableFormat = "^+2500|^+567|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200"
        iUltimo = xaApurosCx.UpperBound(1)
        For iLinhas = 0 To iUltimo
            sRecord = xaApurosCx.value(iLinhas, 0) & "|" & _
                      xaApurosCx.value(iLinhas, 1) & "|" & _
                      Format(xaApurosCx.value(iLinhas, 2), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(xaApurosCx.value(iLinhas, 3), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(xaApurosCx.value(iLinhas, 4), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(xaApurosCx.value(iLinhas, 5), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(xaApurosCx.value(iLinhas, 6), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(xaApurosCx.value(iLinhas, 7), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      xaApurosCx.value(iLinhas, 8) & "|"
            If iLinhas = iUltimo Then
                sTableHeader = sRecord
                .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
            Else
                .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True
            End If

        Next iLinhas

        If Right$(lblApurosCX(2).Caption, 10) < dDataConv() Then
            sRecord = "Total EUR" & "|" & _
                      "|" & _
                      Format(Round(xaApurosCx.value(iUltimo, 2) / 200.482, 2), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(Round(xaApurosCx.value(iUltimo, 3) / 200.482, 2), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(Round(xaApurosCx.value(iUltimo, 4) / 200.482, 2), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(Round(xaApurosCx.value(iUltimo, 5) / 200.482, 2), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(Round(xaApurosCx.value(iUltimo, 6) / 200.482, 2), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      "|" & _
                      "|"
        Else
            sRecord = "Total ESC" & "|" & _
                      "|" & _
                      Format(Round(xaApurosCx.value(iUltimo, 2) * 200.482, 2), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(Round(xaApurosCx.value(iUltimo, 3) * 200.482, 2), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(Round(xaApurosCx.value(iUltimo, 4) * 200.482, 2), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(Round(xaApurosCx.value(iUltimo, 5) * 200.482, 2), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(Round(xaApurosCx.value(iUltimo, 6) * 200.482, 2), "Standard") & "|" & _
                      "|" & _
                      "|"
        End If

        sTableHeader = sRecord
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        .EndDoc
    End With

    frmPrintPreview.Show vbModal
    GoTo Fim

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ImpApuroCx()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Fim:
    Unload frmPrintPreview
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    vspImpressao.KillDoc
End Sub

' impressao dos movimentos Apuros
Private Sub ImpApuroMov()
    Dim vspImpressao As vsPrinter
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sTitulo As String

    On Error GoTo erro

    With frmPrintPreview
        .impressora = ImpressoraListagens
    End With
    Set vspImpressao = frmPrintPreview.vspPreview

    sTitulo = ":"
    If frmPosMain.datApuroGeral.Recordset!xTipo = "Vendas (Global)" Then
        sTitulo = sTitulo & " Todas as Vendas"
    Else
        sTitulo = sTitulo & datApuroGeral.Recordset!xTipo
    End If
    If frmPosMain.datApuroGeral.Recordset!xCaixa = "Global" Then
        sTitulo = sTitulo & " para todas as Caixas"
    Else
        sTitulo = sTitulo & " para a " & datApuroGeral.Recordset!xCaixa
    End If
    sTitulo = sTitulo & " no intervalo de " & datApuroGeral.Recordset!cabapDataInicio & " ate " & datApuroGeral.Recordset!cabapdatafim

    If ImpApuroMovValoresCaixa(vspImpressao, sTitulo) Then GoTo Abortar
    If ImpApuroMovValesCaixa(vspImpressao, sTitulo) Then GoTo Abortar
    If ImpApuroMovMovimentosCaixa(vspImpressao, sTitulo) Then GoTo Abortar
    vspImpressao.EndDoc
    frmPrintPreview.Show vbModal

    GoTo Fim

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ImpApuroMov()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Fim:
    Unload frmPrintPreview
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    vspImpressao.KillDoc
End Sub

' Impressao mov. apuros valores de caixa
Private Function ImpApuroMovValoresCaixa(ByRef vspImpressao As vsPrinter, ByVal sTitulo As String) As Boolean
    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sTableFormat As String, sTableHeader As String
    Dim f As String, s As String
    Dim sNomeListagem As String
    sNomeListagem = "Listagem Mov.Apuros: Valores de Caixa" & sTitulo
    With vspImpressao
        .PageBorder = pbBottom
        .FontName = "Arial"
        .FontSize = 10
        .FontBold = False
        .FontItalic = False
        .HdrFontName = "Arial"
        .HdrFontSize = 9
        .HdrFontBold = False
        .HdrFontItalic = False
        .Footer = sNomeListagem & "|| Página %d"
        .MarginTop = 600
        .MarginBottom = 650
        .MarginLeft = 600
        .MarginRight = 600
        .TextAlign = taLeftBaseline
        .TextAngle = 0
        .CurrentX = 300
        .Preview = True
    End With


    With vspImpressao
        .Orientation = orLandscape
        .StartDoc
        
        ImpressaoDoCabecalho vspImpressao, ImpressoraListagens

        .FontSize = 10
        .FontBold = True
        .MarginLeft = 5000
        .Measure = sNomeListagem
        .CurrentY = 2750 - .TextHei
        .CurrentX = 5000
        .Text = sNomeListagem
        .FontBold = False

        .CurrentY = PosicaoY(.CurrentY + 400)
        .FontSize = 9
        .MarginLeft = 100
        .MarginRight = 100
        sTableFormat = "^+5000"
        sTableHeader = "Entradas"
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        .AutoRTF = True

        f = "3000|>+2000"
        s = ";{ Numerario         }|{" & lblApurosMovCx(0).Caption & "}" & _
            ";{ Cheques           }|{" & lblApurosMovCx(1).Caption & "}" & _
            ";{ Pré-Datados       }|{" & lblApurosMovCx(2).Caption & "}" & _
            ";{ Multibanco        }|{" & lblApurosMovCx(3).Caption & "}" & _
            ";{ Cartões de Crédito}|{" & lblApurosMovCx(4).Caption & "}" & _
            ";{ Pag.Notas Crédito }|{" & lblApurosMovCx(13).Caption & "}" & _
            ";{ Pag. Vales Caixa  }|{" & lblApurosMovCx(5).Caption & "}"

        .Table = f & s

        sTableHeader = "Saidas"
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        s = ";{ Vales de Caixa    }|{" & lblApurosMovCx(8).Caption & "}" & _
            ";{ Pagamentos        }|{" & lblApurosMovCx(6).Caption & "}" & _
            ";{ Notas de Crédito  }|{" & lblApurosMovCx(7).Caption & "}" & _
            ";{" & Space(5) & "}|{" & Space(5) & "}" & _
            ";{ Total de Caixa    }|{" & lblApurosMovCx(10).Caption & "}" & _
            ";{ Nº Vendas         }|{" & lblApurosMovCx(9).Caption & "}" & _
            ";{ Apuro de Caixa    }|{" & lblApurosMovCx(11).Caption & "}" & _
            ";{ Diferença de Caixa}|{" & lblApurosMovCx(12).Caption & "}"

        .Table = f & s

    End With

    Exit Function
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ImpApuroMovValoresCaixa()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Fim:
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    ImpApuroMovValoresCaixa = True
End Function

' impressao dos mov. de apuros de vales de caixa
Private Function ImpApuroMovValesCaixa(ByRef vspImpressao As vsPrinter, ByVal sTitulo As String) As Boolean
    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sTableFormat As String, sTableHeader As String
    Dim sRecord As String
    Dim rsImpressao As Recordset
    Dim dTotalValor As Double
    Dim sNomeListagem As String

    Set rsImpressao = datApurosVales.Recordset.Clone
    If rsImpressao.RecordCount = 0 Then
        Exit Function
    End If

    sNomeListagem = "Listagem Mov.Apuros: Vales de Caixa" & sTitulo
    With vspImpressao
        .NewPage
        .Footer = sNomeListagem & "|| Página %d"
        
        ImpressaoDoCabecalho vspImpressao, ImpressoraListagens

        .FontSize = 10
        .FontBold = True
        .MarginLeft = 5000
        .Measure = sNomeListagem
        .CurrentY = 2750 - .TextHei
        .CurrentX = 5000
        .Text = sNomeListagem
        .FontBold = False

        .CurrentY = PosicaoY(.CurrentY + 400)
        .MarginLeft = 100
        .MarginRight = 100
        .FontSize = 8
        sTableFormat = "^+817|^+2000|^+1500|^+1200|^+3000|^+2000|^+847|^+2000"
        sTableHeader = "Numero|Data Emissão|Operador|Valor|Observações|Entregue a...|Estado|Data de Pagamento"

        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        sTableFormat = "^+817|^+2000|<+1500|>+1200|<+3000|<+2000|<+847|^+2000"

        rsImpressao.MoveFirst
        Do While Not rsImpressao.EOF
            sRecord = rsImpressao!valNumero & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!valDataHora & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!xOperador & "|" & _
                      Format(rsImpressao!valValor, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!valObservacoes & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!xOperadorPaga & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!xEstado & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!valDataHoraPago & "|"

            .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True

            dTotalValor = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!valValor) + dTotalValor
            rsImpressao.MoveNext
        Loop
        .FontBold = True
        sTableFormat = "^+817|^+2000|^+1500|>+1200|^+3000|^+2000|^+847|^+2000"
        sTableHeader = "||Totais|" & Format(dTotalValor, "Standard")
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        .FontBold = False

    End With

    Exit Function
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ImpApuroMovValesCaixa()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Fim:
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    ImpApuroMovValesCaixa = True
End Function

' impressao dos mov. de apuros de Mov. de caixa
Private Function ImpApuroMovMovimentosCaixa(ByRef vspImpressao As vsPrinter, ByVal sTitulo As String) As Boolean

    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sTableFormat As String, sTableHeader As String
    Dim sRecord As String
    Dim rsImpressao As Recordset
    Dim dTotalCredito As Double, dTotalDebito As Double
    Dim sNomeListagem As String

    Set rsImpressao = datApurosMovimentos.Recordset.Clone
    If rsImpressao.RecordCount = 0 Then
        Exit Function
    End If
    sNomeListagem = "Listagem Mov.Apuros: Movimentos de Caixa" & sTitulo
    With vspImpressao
        .NewPage
        .HdrFontSize = 9
        .Footer = sNomeListagem & "|| Página %d"
        
        ImpressaoDoCabecalho vspImpressao, ImpressoraListagens
        
        .FontSize = 10
        .FontBold = True
        .MarginLeft = 5000
        .Measure = sNomeListagem
        .CurrentY = 2750 - .TextHei
        .CurrentX = 5000
        .Text = sNomeListagem
        .FontBold = False

        .CurrentY = PosicaoY(.CurrentY + 400)
        .FontSize = 9
        .MarginLeft = 100
        .MarginRight = 100
        .FontSize = 8
        sTableFormat = "^+2000|^+4000|^+1200|^+1200|^+1200"
        sTableHeader = "Codigo|Descrição|NºDoc.|Debito|Credito"

        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        sTableFormat = "^+2000|<+4000|^+1200|>+1200|>+1200"
        rsImpressao.MoveFirst
        Do While Not rsImpressao.EOF
            sRecord = rsImpressao!tbmvCodigo & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!mcxMovimentoDescricao & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!mcxNumDoc & "|" & _
                      Format(rsImpressao!xDebito, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format(rsImpressao!xCredito, "Standard") & "|"

            .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True

            dTotalDebito = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!xDebito) + dTotalDebito
            dTotalCredito = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!xCredito) + dTotalCredito
            rsImpressao.MoveNext
        Loop
        .FontBold = True
        sTableFormat = "^+2000|^+4000|^+1200|>+1200|>+1200"
        sTableHeader = "||Totais|" & Format(dTotalDebito, "Standard") & "|" & Format(dTotalCredito, "Standard")
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        sTableHeader = "||Saldo||" & Format(oUtils.Convert2Double(lblApurosMov(0).Caption), "Standard")
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
    End With

    Exit Function
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ImpApuroMovMovimentosCaixa()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Fim:
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    ImpApuroMovMovimentosCaixa = True
End Function


' Impressao dos movimentos de Caixa
Private Sub ImpCxMovimentos()
    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sTableFormat As String, sTableHeader As String
    Dim sRecord As String
    Dim dTotalDebito As Double, dTotalCredito As Double
    Dim vspImpressao As vsPrinter
    Dim rsImpressao As Recordset
    Dim sNomeListagem As String

    With frmPrintPreview
        .impressora = ImpressoraListagens
    End With
    Set vspImpressao = frmPrintPreview.vspPreview

    Set rsImpressao = datCaixaMov.Recordset.Clone
    sNomeListagem = "Listagem de Movimentos da Caixa: " & datCaixa.Recordset!cxNome & " da data de " & datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlcxDataAbertura
    With vspImpressao
        .PageBorder = pbBottom
        .FontName = "Arial"
        .FontSize = 8
        .FontBold = False
        .FontItalic = False
        .HdrFontName = "Arial"
        .HdrFontSize = 8
        .HdrFontBold = False
        .HdrFontItalic = False
        .Footer = sNomeListagem & "| Página %d"
        .MarginTop = 600
        .MarginBottom = 650
        .MarginLeft = 600
        .MarginRight = 600
        .TextAlign = taLeftBaseline
        .TextAngle = 0
        .CurrentX = 300
        .Preview = True
    End With
    With vspImpressao
        .Orientation = orPortrait
        .StartDoc
        
        ImpressaoDoCabecalho vspImpressao, ImpressoraListagens
        
        .FontSize = 10
        .FontBold = True
        .MarginLeft = 5000
        .Measure = sNomeListagem
        .CurrentY = 2750 - .TextHei
        .CurrentX = 5000
        .Text = sNomeListagem
        .FontBold = False
        .CurrentY = PosicaoY(.CurrentY + 400)
        .MarginLeft = 100
        .MarginRight = 100
        .FontSize = 8
        sTableFormat = "^+1000|^+3100|^+3100|^+900|^+900|^+900|^+900"
        sTableHeader = "Codigo|Descrição|Observações|Numero|Debito|Credito|Nº Cli"

        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        sTableFormat = "^+1000|<+3100|<+3100|^+900|>+900|>+900|^+900"
        rsImpressao.MoveFirst


        Do While Not rsImpressao.EOF

            Dim NumCliente As Long

            If IsNull(rsImpressao!NumCliente) Then
                If IsNull(rsImpressao!cliNumero) Then
                    NumCliente = 0
                Else
                    NumCliente = rsImpressao!cliNumero
                End If
            Else
                NumCliente = rsImpressao!NumCliente
            End If

            sRecord = rsImpressao!tbmvCodigo & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!mcxMovimentoDescricao & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!mcxObservacoes & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!mcxNumDoc & "|" & _
                      Format$(rsImpressao!xDebito, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      Format$(rsImpressao!xCredito, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      NumCliente
            .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True
            dTotalDebito = dTotalDebito + oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!xDebito)
            dTotalCredito = dTotalCredito + oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!xCredito)
            rsImpressao.MoveNext

        Loop
        .FontBold = True
        sTableFormat = "^+1000|^+3100|^+3100|^+900|>+900|>+900|^+900"

        sTableHeader = "||Totais" & MoedaListagem(True) & "||" & Format(dTotalDebito, "Standard") & "|" & Format(dTotalCredito, "Standard")
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        sTableHeader = "||Totais" & MoedaListagem(False) & "||" & ConvertMoeda(dTotalDebito, , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(dTotalCredito, , , False)
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        sTableFormat = "^+1000|^+3100|^+3100|^+900|^+900|>+900|^+900"
        sTableHeader = "||Saldo" & MoedaListagem(True) & "|||" & Format(lblCxMov(0).Caption, "Standard")
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        sTableHeader = "||Saldo" & MoedaListagem(False) & "|||" & ConvertMoeda(lblCxMov(0).Caption, , , False)
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        .EndDoc
    End With
    frmPrintPreview.Show vbModal
    Set rsImpressao = Nothing
    GoTo Fim
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ImpCxMovimentos()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Fim:
    Unload frmPrintPreview
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    vspImpressao.KillDoc
End Sub

' Impressao dos vales de Caixa
Private Sub ImpCxVales()
    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sTableFormat As String, sTableHeader As String
    Dim sRecord As String
    Dim dTotal As Double
    Dim vspImpressao As vsPrinter
    Dim rsImpressao As Recordset
    Dim sNomeListagem As String

    With frmPrintPreview
        .impressora = ImpressoraListagens
    End With
    Set vspImpressao = frmPrintPreview.vspPreview

    Set rsImpressao = datCaixaVales.Recordset.Clone
    sNomeListagem = "Listagem dos Vales da Caixa: " & datCaixa.Recordset!cxNome & " à data de " & datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlcxDataAbertura
    With vspImpressao
        .PageBorder = pbBottom
        .FontName = "Arial"
        .FontSize = 9
        .FontBold = False
        .FontItalic = False
        .HdrFontName = "Arial"
        .HdrFontSize = 9
        .HdrFontBold = False
        .HdrFontItalic = False
        .Footer = sNomeListagem & "| Página %d"
        .MarginTop = 600
        .MarginBottom = 650
        .MarginLeft = 600
        .MarginRight = 600
        .TextAlign = taLeftBaseline
        .TextAngle = 0
        .CurrentX = 300
        .Preview = True
    End With
    With vspImpressao
        .Orientation = orLandscape
        .StartDoc
        
        ImpressaoDoCabecalho vspImpressao, ImpressoraListagens

        .FontSize = 10
        .FontBold = True
        .MarginLeft = 5000
        .Measure = sNomeListagem
        .CurrentY = 2750 - .TextHei
        .CurrentX = 5000
        .Text = sNomeListagem
        .FontBold = False

        .CurrentY = PosicaoY(.CurrentY + 400)
        .MarginLeft = 100
        .MarginRight = 100
        .FontSize = 7
        sTableFormat = "^+900|^+1701|^+1701|^+1200|^+3500|^+1701|^+850|^+1701"
        sTableHeader = "Numero|Data Emissão|Operador|Valor|Observações|Entregue a...|Estado|Data de Pagamento"

        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        sTableFormat = "^+900|^+1701|<+1701|>+1200|<+3500|<+1701|^+850|^+1701"
        rsImpressao.MoveFirst

        Do While Not rsImpressao.EOF
            sRecord = rsImpressao!valNumero & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!valDataHora & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!xOperador & "|" & _
                      Format$(rsImpressao!valValor, "Standard") & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!valObservacoes & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!xOperadorPaga & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!xEstado & "|" & _
                      rsImpressao!valDataHoraPago & "|"

            .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True
            dTotal = dTotal + oUtils.Convert2Double(rsImpressao!valValor)
            rsImpressao.MoveNext

        Loop
        .FontBold = True
        sTableFormat = "^+900|^+1701|^+1701|>+1200|^+3500|^+1701|^+850|^+1701"
        sTableHeader = "||Total|" & Format(dTotal, "Standard")
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        .EndDoc
    End With

    frmPrintPreview.Show vbModal
    Set rsImpressao = Nothing
    GoTo Fim

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ImpCxVales()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Fim:
    Unload frmPrintPreview
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    vspImpressao.KillDoc
End Sub

' Cria o Query para a impressao dos documentos lista
Private Sub IniciaQuery(ByRef strQuery As String, ByVal dData1 As Date, ByVal dData2 As Date)

    Dim iposCbo1 As Integer
    Dim strCampo As String
    Dim sAuxData As Date

    If dData1 > dData2 Then
        sAuxData = dData2
        dData2 = dData1
        dData1 = sAuxData
    End If

    iposCbo1 = cboDoc(1).ListIndex
    Select Case iposCbo1
        Case 1, 2
            strQuery = "Select * From qyLstRelacaoFacturasDoc"
        Case 3, 4
            strQuery = "Select * From qyLstRelacaoFacturasNTNC"
    End Select

    strCampo = ""

    Select Case cboDoc(2).ListIndex
        Case 1    ' Numero de documento
            If txtDoc(1).Visible And oUtils.Convert2Long(txtDoc(1).Text) <> 0 Then
                strCampo = "cabdocNumDoc >= " & oUtils.Convert2Long(txtDoc(0).Text) & " and cabdocNumDoc <= " & oUtils.Convert2Long(txtDoc(1).Text) & " and "
            Else
                strCampo = "cabdocNumDoc = " & oUtils.Convert2Long(txtDoc(0).Text) & " and "
            End If

        Case 2    ' Numero de Nif
            strCampo = "cabposNif = " & "'" & Trim(txtDoc(0).Text) & "' and "

        Case 3    ' Nome do cliente
            strCampo = "cabposNome = " & "'" & Trim(txtDoc(0).Text) & "' and "
    End Select
    strCampo = strCampo & "cabdocData >= #" & Format(dData1, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "# and cabdocData <= #" & Format(dData2, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "#"

    If chkDoc(0).value = 1 And chkDoc(1).value = 1 Then
        strQuery = strQuery & " WHERE cabdocTipoDoc = " & iposCbo1 & " and " & strCampo

    ElseIf chkDoc(0).value = 1 And chkDoc(1).value = 0 Then
        strQuery = strQuery & " WHERE cabdocTipoDoc = " & iposCbo1 & " and " & strCampo

    ElseIf chkDoc(0).value = 0 And chkDoc(1).value = 1 Then
        strQuery = "SELECT * FROM qyLstRelacaoFacturasDoc WHERE " & strCampo _
                   & " UNION " _
                   & " SELECT * FROM qyLstRelacaoFacturasNTNC WHERE " & strCampo

    ElseIf chkDoc(0).value = 0 And chkDoc(1).value = 0 Then
        strQuery = "Select * From qyLstRelacaoFacturasDoc UNION Select * From qyLstRelacaoFacturasNTNC"

    End If


End Sub

' impressao da lista dos documentos
Private Sub ImprimirDocLista(ByVal iAno As Integer, ByVal strQuery As String)

    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sTableFormat As String, sTableHeader As String
    Dim sRecord As String, sDoc As String, sTitulo As String, dData As String
    Dim vspImpressao As vsPrinter
    Dim iRR As Integer
    Dim aTotaisDoc(0 To 7) As Double, aTotaisDias(0 To 7) As Double
    Dim aTotalGeral(0 To 7) As Double, aEscalaoIVA(0 To 3) As Variant
    Dim sIva(0 To 3) As String
    Dim bFirstDoc As Boolean, bFirstDias As Boolean, bCarregaImpressao As Boolean
    Dim rsImpressao As Recordset
    Dim QdfImp As QueryDef
    Dim sNomeListagem As String
    Dim sSerie As String
    
    Dim mostraSerie As Boolean: mostraSerie = ObtemSettingBool("DocsVenda_MostraSerie")

    sIva(0) = "": sIva(1) = "": sIva(2) = "": sIva(3) = ""

    oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, "Select * From qyIva Where ivaAno = " & iAno, rsImpressao, dbOpenSnapshot
    If rsImpressao.RecordCount > 0 Then
        rsImpressao.MoveLast
        rsImpressao.MoveFirst
        For iRR = 0 To 3
            With rsImpressao
                If Not .EOF Then
                    aEscalaoIVA(iRR) = !IvaPercentagem
                    .MoveNext
                Else
                    aEscalaoIVA(iRR) = 0
                End If
            End With
        Next iRR
        Set rsImpressao = Nothing
    End If
    With frmPrintPreview
        .impressora = ImpressoraListagens
    End With
    Set vspImpressao = frmPrintPreview.vspPreview

    sTitulo = IIf(chkDoc(0).value = 1, "do Tipo " & cboDoc(1).Text, "")
    If chkDoc(1).value = 1 Then
        Select Case cboDoc(2).ListIndex
            Case 1    ' Numero Doc
                If txtDoc(1).Visible Then
                    sTitulo = sTitulo & " entre o Numero Doc. " & txtDoc(0).Text & " ate ao Numero Doc. " & txtDoc(1).Text
                Else
                    sTitulo = sTitulo & " com numero Doc. igual a " & txtDoc(0).Text
                End If
            Case 2    ' Numero de NIF
                sTitulo = sTitulo & " com Numero NIF. igual a " & txtDoc(0).Text
            Case 3    ' Nome
                sTitulo = sTitulo & " com o Nome igual a " & txtDoc(0).Text
            Case 4    ' Data
                sTitulo = sTitulo & " Referente ao periodo " & txtDoc(0).Text
        End Select

    End If

    Set QdfImp = dbOptiware98.CreateQueryDef("")
    With QdfImp
        .sql = strQuery
        .parameters("ivaEscalao1") = aEscalaoIVA(0)
        .parameters("ivaEscalao2") = aEscalaoIVA(1)
        .parameters("ivaEscalao3") = aEscalaoIVA(2)
        .parameters("ivaEscalao4") = aEscalaoIVA(3)
        Set rsImpressao = .OpenRecordset(dbOpenSnapshot)
    End With


    If rsImpressao.RecordCount <= 0 Then
        MsgBox "Não existem dados para o critério indicado!", vbInformation
        Set rsImpressao = Nothing
        GoTo Fim
    End If
    bFirstDoc = True
    bFirstDias = True

    For iRR = 0 To 6
        aTotalGeral(iRR) = 0
    Next iRR
    For iRR = 0 To 6
        aTotaisDoc(iRR) = 0
    Next iRR
    For iRR = 0 To 6
        aTotaisDias(iRR) = 0
    Next iRR
    sNomeListagem = "Listagem de Documentos " & sTitulo
    With vspImpressao
        .PageBorder = pbBottom
        .FontName = "Arial"
        .FontSize = 6
        .FontBold = False
        .FontItalic = False
        .HdrFontName = "Arial"
        .HdrFontSize = 7
        .HdrFontBold = False
        .HdrFontItalic = False
        .Footer = sNomeListagem & "| Página %d"
        .MarginTop = 600
        .MarginBottom = 650
        .MarginLeft = 600
        .MarginRight = 300
        .TextAlign = taLeftBaseline
        .TextAngle = 0
        .CurrentX = 300
        .Preview = True
    End With
    With vspImpressao
        .Orientation = orLandscape
        .StartDoc
        
        ImpressaoDoCabecalho vspImpressao, ImpressoraListagens

        .FontSize = 10
        .FontBold = True
        .MarginLeft = 5000
        .Measure = sNomeListagem
        .CurrentY = 2750 - .TextHei
        .CurrentX = 5000
        .Text = sNomeListagem
        .FontBold = False
        .CurrentY = PosicaoY(.CurrentY + 400)
        .MarginLeft = 100
        .MarginRight = 100
        .FontSize = 6

        sTableFormat = "^+1100|^+847|^+847|^+2900|^+1130|^+1130|^+1130"
        If aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0 Then sIva(0) = "|^+1130"
        If aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0 Then sIva(1) = "|^+1130"
        If aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0 Then sIva(2) = "|^+1130"
        If aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0 Then sIva(3) = "|^+1130"
        sTableFormat = sTableFormat & sIva(0) & sIva(1) & sIva(2) & sIva(3) & "|^+1130|^+847"

        sTableHeader = "Tipo|Data|Número|Nome de Cliente|Descontos|Comp.|Valor Total"
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0, "|Iva " & aEscalaoIVA(0), "")
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0, "|Iva " & aEscalaoIVA(1), "")
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0, "|Iva " & aEscalaoIVA(2), "")
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0, "|Iva " & aEscalaoIVA(3), "")
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & "|Valor do IVA|Estado"

        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        sTableFormat = "^+1100|^+847|^+847|<+2900|>+1130|>+1130|>+1130"
        If aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0 Then sIva(0) = "|>+1130"
        If aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0 Then sIva(1) = "|>+1130"
        If aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0 Then sIva(2) = "|>+1130"
        If aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0 Then sIva(3) = "|>+1130"
        sTableFormat = sTableFormat & sIva(0) & sIva(1) & sIva(2) & sIva(3) & "|>+1130|^+847"

        rsImpressao.MoveFirst
        sDoc = "" & rsImpressao!xTipodoc
        dData = rsImpressao!CabdocData
        
        Do While Not rsImpressao.EOF
            If sDoc <> rsImpressao!xTipodoc Then
                .FontBold = True
                sTableFormat = "^+1100|^+847|^+847|^+2900|>+1130|>+1130|>+1130"
                If aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0 Then sIva(0) = "|>+1130"
                If aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0 Then sIva(1) = "|>+1130"
                If aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0 Then sIva(2) = "|>+1130"
                If aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0 Then sIva(3) = "|>+1130"
                sTableFormat = sTableFormat & sIva(0) & sIva(1) & sIva(2) & sIva(3) & "|>+1130|^+847"

                sRecord = "|||Totais de Documentos" & MoedaListagem(True) & "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(0), "Standard") & "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(1), "Standard") & "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(2), "Standard")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(3), "Standard"), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(4), "Standard"), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(5), "standard"), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(6), "standard"), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(7), "Standard")
                .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True

                sRecord = "|||Totais de Documentos" & MoedaListagem(False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(0), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(1), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(2), , , False)
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(3), , , False), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(4), , , False), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(5), , , False), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(6), , , False), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(7), , , False)
                .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True

                .FontBold = False
                sDoc = rsImpressao!xTipodoc
                For iRR = 0 To 6
                    aTotaisDoc(iRR) = 0
                Next iRR
                bFirstDoc = True
                bCarregaImpressao = False
            End If

            If dData <> rsImpressao!CabdocData Then
                .FontBold = True
                sTableFormat = "^+1100|^+847|^+847|^+2900|>+1130|>+1130|>+1130"
                If aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0 Then sIva(0) = "|>+1130"
                If aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0 Then sIva(1) = "|>+1130"
                If aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0 Then sIva(2) = "|>+1130"
                If aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0 Then sIva(3) = "|>+1130"
                sTableFormat = sTableFormat & sIva(0) & sIva(1) & sIva(2) & sIva(3) & "|>+1130|^+847"

                sRecord = "|||Totais de Dia" & MoedaListagem(True) & "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(0), "Standard") & "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(1), "Standard") & "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(2), "Standard")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(3), "Standard"), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(4), "standard"), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(5), "standard"), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(6), "standard"), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(7), "standard")
                .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True

                ' Euros
                sRecord = "|||Totais de Dia" & MoedaListagem(False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(0), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(1), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(2), , , False)
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(3), , , False), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(4), , , False), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(5), , , False), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(6), , , False), "")
                sRecord = sRecord & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(7), , , False)
                .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True

                .FontBold = False
                For iRR = 0 To 6
                    aTotaisDias(iRR) = 0
                Next iRR
                dData = rsImpressao!CabdocData
                bFirstDias = True
                bFirstDoc = True
                bCarregaImpressao = False
            End If

            If bCarregaImpressao Then
                sTableFormat = "^+1100|^+847|^+847|<+2900|>+1130|>+1130|>+1130"
                If aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0 Then sIva(0) = "|>+1130"
                If aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0 Then sIva(1) = "|>+1130"
                If aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0 Then sIva(2) = "|>+1130"
                If aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0 Then sIva(3) = "|>+1130"
                sTableFormat = sTableFormat & sIva(0) & sIva(1) & sIva(2) & sIva(3) & "|>+1130|^+847"

                sRecord = IIf(bFirstDoc, sDoc, "") & "|" & _
                          IIf(bFirstDias, dData, "") & "|" & _
                          rsImpressao!CabDocNumDoc & "|" & _
                          rsImpressao!cabposNome & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!cabdocTotDesconto, "Standard") & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!cabdocTotComp, "Standard") & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!CabDocTotal - rsImpressao!cabdocTotDesconto, "Standard") & "|" & _
                          IIf(aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0, Format$(rsImpressao!iva1, "Standard") & "|", "") & _
                          IIf(aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0, Format$(rsImpressao!Iva2, "Standard") & "|", "") & _
                          IIf(aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0, Format$(rsImpressao!iva3, "Standard") & "|", "") & _
                          IIf(aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0, Format$(rsImpressao!Iva4, "Standard") & "|", "") & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!cabdocTotalIva, "Standard") & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!xEstado, "Standard")
                bFirstDoc = False
                bFirstDias = False
                If LCase(Trim$(rsImpressao!xEstado)) <> Doc_Anulados Then
                    aTotalGeral(0) = rsImpressao!cabdocTotDesconto + aTotalGeral(0): aTotalGeral(1) = rsImpressao!cabdocTotComp + aTotalGeral(1)
                    aTotalGeral(2) = rsImpressao!CabDocTotal + aTotalGeral(2) - rsImpressao!cabdocTotDesconto: aTotalGeral(3) = rsImpressao!iva1 + aTotalGeral(3)
                    aTotalGeral(4) = rsImpressao!Iva2 + aTotalGeral(4): aTotalGeral(5) = rsImpressao!iva3 + aTotalGeral(5)
                    aTotalGeral(6) = rsImpressao!Iva4 + aTotalGeral(6): aTotalGeral(7) = rsImpressao!cabdocTotalIva + aTotalGeral(7)

                    aTotaisDoc(0) = rsImpressao!cabdocTotDesconto + aTotaisDoc(0): aTotaisDoc(1) = rsImpressao!cabdocTotComp + aTotaisDoc(1)
                    aTotaisDoc(2) = rsImpressao!CabDocTotal + aTotaisDoc(2) - rsImpressao!cabdocTotDesconto: aTotaisDoc(3) = rsImpressao!iva1 + aTotaisDoc(3)
                    aTotaisDoc(4) = rsImpressao!Iva2 + aTotaisDoc(4): aTotaisDoc(5) = rsImpressao!iva3 + aTotaisDoc(5)
                    aTotaisDoc(6) = rsImpressao!Iva4 + aTotaisDoc(6): aTotaisDoc(7) = rsImpressao!cabdocTotalIva + aTotaisDoc(7)

                    aTotaisDias(0) = rsImpressao!cabdocTotDesconto + aTotaisDias(0): aTotaisDias(1) = rsImpressao!cabdocTotComp + aTotaisDias(1)
                    aTotaisDias(2) = rsImpressao!CabDocTotal + aTotaisDias(2) - rsImpressao!cabdocTotDesconto: aTotaisDias(3) = rsImpressao!iva1 + aTotaisDias(3)
                    aTotaisDias(4) = rsImpressao!Iva2 + aTotaisDias(4): aTotaisDias(5) = rsImpressao!iva3 + aTotaisDias(5)
                    aTotaisDias(6) = rsImpressao!Iva4 + aTotaisDias(6): aTotaisDias(7) = rsImpressao!cabdocTotalIva + aTotaisDias(7)
                End If
                .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True
                rsImpressao.MoveNext

            End If
            bCarregaImpressao = True
        Loop
        .FontBold = True
        sTableFormat = "^+1100|^+847|^+847|^+2900|>+1130|>+1130|>+1130"
        If aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0 Then sIva(0) = "|>+1130"
        If aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0 Then sIva(1) = "|>+1130"
        If aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0 Then sIva(2) = "|>+1130"
        If aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0 Then sIva(3) = "|>+1130"
        sTableFormat = sTableFormat & sIva(0) & sIva(1) & sIva(2) & sIva(3) & "|>+1130|^+847"

        sRecord = "|||Totais de Documentos" & MoedaListagem(True) & "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(0), "Standard") & "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(1), "Standard") & "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(2), "Standard")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(3), "Standard"), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(4), "Standard"), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(5), "standard"), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(6), "standard"), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & "|" & Format(aTotaisDoc(7), "Standard")
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True

        sRecord = "|||Totais de Documentos" & MoedaListagem(False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(0), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(1), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(2), , , False)
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(3), , , False), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(4), , , False), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(5), , , False), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(6), , , False), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDoc(7), , , False)
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True

        sRecord = "|||Totais de Dia" & MoedaListagem(True) & "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(0), "Standard") & "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(1), "Standard") & "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(2), "Standard")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(3), "Standard"), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(4), "standard"), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(5), "standard"), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(6), "standard"), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & "|" & Format(aTotaisDias(7), "standard")
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True

        ' Euros
        sRecord = "|||Totais de Dia" & MoedaListagem(False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(0), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(1), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(2), , , False)
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(3), , , False), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(4), , , False), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(5), , , False), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(6), , , False), "")
        sRecord = sRecord & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotaisDias(7), , , False)
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, 0, True

        sTableHeader = "|||Totais Gerais" & MoedaListagem(True) & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(0), "Standard") & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(1), "standard") & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(2), "standard")
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(3), "standard"), "")
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(4), "standard"), "")
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(5), "standard"), "")
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0, "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(6), "standard"), "")
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & "|" & Format(aTotalGeral(7), "standard")
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        sTableHeader = "|||Totais Gerais" & MoedaListagem(False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(0), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(1), , , False) & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(2), , , False)
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(0) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(3), , , False), "")
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(1) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(4), , , False), "")
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(2) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(5), , , False), "")
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & IIf(aEscalaoIVA(3) > 0, "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(6), , , False), "")
        sTableHeader = sTableHeader & "|" & ConvertMoeda(aTotalGeral(7), , , False)
        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        .EndDoc

    End With

    frmPrintPreview.Show vbModal

    GoTo Fim

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ImprimirDocLista()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Fim:
    Unload frmPrintPreview
Abortar:      On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    vspImpressao.KillDoc
End Sub

' impressao das vendas Detalhas
' aTotaisFamilias(0); aTotaisGeral(0) -> Quantidade
' aTotaisFamilias(1); aTotaisGeral(1) -> IVA
' aTotaisFamilias(2); aTotaisGeral(2) -> Desconto
' aTotaisFamilias(3); aTotaisGeral(3) -> Comparticipa
' aTotaisFamilias(4); aTotaisGeral(4) -> Valor

Private Sub ImprimirCxVendasDetalhadas()

    Dim fFirst As Boolean

    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim iCount As Integer

    Dim sTableFormat As String
    Dim sTableHeader As String
    Dim sRecord As String
    Dim sFamilia As String
    Dim sData As String
    Dim sTitulo As String
    Dim sFieldName As String

    Dim dComissaoLO As Double
    Dim dComissaoLC As Double
    Dim dComissaoAros As Double
    Dim dComissaoOculosSol As Double
    Dim dComissaoOutros As Double
    Dim dComissaoTaxa As Double
    Dim dComissaoValor As Double

    Dim aTotaisFamilias(0 To 5) As Double
    Dim aTotalGeral(0 To 5) As Double

    Dim vspImpressao As vsPrinter
    Dim rsImpressao As Recordset
    Dim rsUtilizadores As Recordset

    On Error GoTo erro

    'Objecto de impressão
    With frmPrintPreview
        .impressora = ImpressoraListagens
    End With
    Set vspImpressao = frmPrintPreview.vspPreview

    'Título da Listagem
    sTitulo = cboCxVendasGeral(0).Text
    sData = lblCxVendasGeral(0).Caption
    'Dados da Listagem
    Set rsImpressao = datCxVendasGeral(0).Recordset

    'Dados dos Utilizadores
    Set rsUtilizadores = dbo.OpenRecordset("Utilizadores", dbOpenTable)
    With rsUtilizadores
        If (.RecordCount > 0) Then
            .Index = "PrimaryKey"
        End If
    End With

    'Inicialização de variáveis
    fFirst = True
    For iCount = 0 To 5
        aTotaisFamilias(iCount) = 0
    Next iCount
    For iCount = 0 To 5
        aTotalGeral(iCount) = 0
    Next iCount
    dComissaoLO = 0
    dComissaoLC = 0
    dComissaoAros = 0
    dComissaoOculosSol = 0
    dComissaoOutros = 0

    With vspImpressao

        'Definição das características da listagem
        .PageBorder = pbBottom
        .FontName = "Arial"
        .FontSize = 7
        .FontBold = False
        .FontItalic = False
        .HdrFontName = "Arial"
        .HdrFontSize = 7
        .HdrFontBold = False
        .HdrFontItalic = False
        .Footer = "Listagem de Vendas Por " & sTitulo & " Referente à Data de " & sData & "| Página %d"
        .MarginTop = 500
        .MarginBottom = 650
        .MarginLeft = 500
        .MarginRight = 500
        .TextAlign = taLeftBaseline
        .TextAngle = 0
        .CurrentX = 500
        .Preview = True
        .Orientation = orLandscape
        .StartDoc
        .CurrentX = 500: .Text = "Listagem de Vendas Por " & sTitulo & " Referente à Data de " & sData
        .CurrentY = PosicaoY(.CurrentY + 200)
        .MarginLeft = 500
        .MarginRight = 500
        .FontSize = 7

        'Cabeçalho das colunas
        sTableFormat = "^+1985|^+1530|^+2552|^+850|^+1200|^+1200|^+1200|^+1300|^+1200"
        sTableHeader = tdgCxVendasGeral.Columns(0).Caption & "|Referencia|Descrição|Qt.|T. Valor|T. Iva|T. Desconto|T. Comparticipação|Preço Médio"

        'Acrescentar colunas da comissão se for a listagem por operador
        If (sTitulo = "Operador") Then
            sTableFormat = sTableFormat & "|^+800|^+1200"
            sTableHeader = sTableHeader & "|Comissão|Valor Comissão"
        End If

        .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0
        sTableFormat = "<+1985|^+1530|<+2552|^+850|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200"

        'Acrescentar colunas da comissão se for a listagem por operador
        If (sTitulo = "Operador") Then
            sTableFormat = sTableFormat & "^+800|^+1200"
        End If

        rsImpressao.MoveFirst


        'Comissões para o utilizador
        If (sTitulo = "Operador") Then
            sFieldName = "Utilizador"
            If (rsUtilizadores.RecordCount > 0) Then
                rsUtilizadores.Seek "=", rsImpressao!UtilizadorID
                If rsUtilizadores.NoMatch Then
                    dComissaoLO = 0
                    dComissaoLC = 0
                    dComissaoAros = 0
                    dComissaoOculosSol = 0
                    dComissaoOutros = 0
                Else
                    dComissaoLO = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsUtilizadores!usrComissaoLO)
                    dComissaoLC = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsUtilizadores!usrComissaoLC)
                    dComissaoAros = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsUtilizadores!usrComissaoAros)
                    dComissaoOculosSol = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsUtilizadores!usrComissaoOculosSol)
                    dComissaoOutros = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsUtilizadores!usrComissaoOutros)
                End If
            End If
        Else
            sFieldName = "Familia"
        End If

        sFamilia = rsImpressao.fields(sFieldName) & vbNullString

        Do While Not rsImpressao.EOF

            'Imprimir Totais se mudar de Família / Operador
            If (sFamilia <> rsImpressao.fields(sFieldName)) Then
                sTableFormat = "<+1985|^+1530|^+2552|^+850|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1300|>+1200"

                .FontBold = True
                sRecord = "||Totais de " & sTitulo & "|" & _
                          aTotaisFamilias(0) & "|" & _
                          Format$(aTotaisFamilias(4), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & _
                          Format$(aTotaisFamilias(1), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & _
                          Format$(aTotaisFamilias(2), "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & _
                          Format$(aTotaisFamilias(3), "###,###,##0.00")

                'Acrescentar colunas da comissão se for a listagem por operador
                If (sTitulo = "Operador") Then
                    sTableFormat = sTableFormat & "|>+800|>+1200"
                    sRecord = sRecord & "||" & Format$(aTotaisFamilias(5), "###,###,##0.00")
                End If

                .AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, sRecord, &HE0E0E0, &HE0E0E0, True
                .FontBold = False

                sFamilia = rsImpressao.fields(sFieldName)

                For iCount = 0 To 5
                    aTotaisFamilias(iCount) = 0
                Next iCount
                fFirst = True

                'Comissões para o utilizador
                If (sTitulo = "Operador") Then
                    If (rsUtilizadores.RecordCount > 0) Then
                        rsUtilizadores.Seek "=", rsImpressao!UtilizadorID
                        If rsUtilizadores.NoMatch Then
                            dComissaoLO = 0
                            dComissaoLC = 0
                            dComissaoAros = 0
                            dComissaoOculosSol = 0
                            dComissaoOutros = 0
                        Else
                            dComissaoLO = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsUtilizadores!usrComissaoLO)
                            dComissaoLC = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsUtilizadores!usrComissaoLC)
                            dComissaoAros = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsUtilizadores!usrComissaoAros)
                            dComissaoOculosSol = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsUtilizadores!usrComissaoOculosSol)
                            dComissaoOutros = oUtils.Convert2Double(rsUtilizadores!usrComissaoOutros)
                        End If
                    End If
                End If

            Else

                sTableFormat = "<+1985|^+1530|<+2552|^+850|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1300|>+1200"

                sRecord = IIf(fFirst, sFamilia, vbNullString) & "|" & _
                          rsImpressao!Referencia & "|" & _
                          rsImpressao!descricao & "|" & _
                          rsImpressao!totalquantidade & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!totalvalor, "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!TotalIVA, "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!TotalDescontos, "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!TotalComparticipacao, "###,###,##0.00") & "|" & _
                          Format$(rsImpressao!precomedio, "###,###,##0.00")

                If (sTitulo = "Operador") Then
                    Select Case rsImpressao!Familia & vbNullString
                        Case "Lentes Oftálmicas"
                            dComissaoTaxa = dComissaoLO
                        Case "Lentes de Contacto"
                            dComissaoTaxa = dComissaoLC
                        Case "Aros"
                            dComissaoTaxa = dComissaoAros
                        Case "Óculos de Sol"
                            dComissaoTaxa = dComissaoOculosSol
                        Case Else
                            dComissaoTaxa = dComissaoOutros
                    End Select
