    SsQqLl = "Update ControleCaixa SET ctrlcxApurada = 1 WHERE ctrlcxDataAbertura >= #" & Format(vPeriodo(0), "mm-dd-yyyy") & "# and ctrlcxDataAbertura <= #" & Format(vPeriodo(1), "mm-dd-yyyy") & "#" & IIf(lIdCaixa <> 0, " and ctrlcxCaixaId = " & lIdCaixa, "")

    dbo.Execute SsQqLl

    OptiwareEx.CommitTrans
    fTransaction = False
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "GravaApuroDeCaixa()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:      On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    If fTransaction Then OptiwareEx.RollbackTrans
End Sub

'Calculos de Apuros de Movimentos de Caixa
Private Sub CalculoMovimentosCx(ByVal dData1 As Date, ByVal dData2 As Date)
    Dim xRs As Recordset
    Dim SsQqLl As String, ssqlMovCx As String
    Dim TotApuros As Double
    Dim TotVales As Double
    Dim lidControleCaixa As Long
    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim iErro As Integer
    '    lidControleCaixa = oUtils.Convert2Long(tabCaixa.Tag)
    lidControleCaixa = oUtils.Convert2Long(cboApurosCX(1).Tag)

    If lidControleCaixa <> 0 Then

        SsQqLl = "SELECT * FROM qyVales WHERE valControleCaixaId = "
        oUtils.CreateDataRecordset dbOptiware98, SsQqLl & lidControleCaixa, datApurosVales, dbOpenSnapshot

        SsQqLl = "SELECT * FROM qyMovCxApuros WHERE mcxControleCaixaId = "
        oUtils.CreateDataRecordset dbOptiware98, SsQqLl & lidControleCaixa, datApurosMovimentos, dbOpenSnapshot

        ssqlMovCx = "Select Sum(xCredito)- Sum(xDebito) as XSaldo from qyMovCaixaCxSaldo Where mcxControleCaixaId = " & lidControleCaixa

        SsQqLl = "SELECT SUM(valValor) as [xValor] FROM Qyvales WHERE ((valDataHoraPago) Is Not Null) AND valControleCaixaId = " & lidControleCaixa
    Else
        SsQqLl = "SELECT * FROM qyVales WHERE valControleCaixaId IN (SELECT ctrlcxId FROM ControleCaixa WHERE ctrlcxDataAbertura BetWeen #" & Format(dData1, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "# And #" & Format(dData2, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "#)"
        oUtils.CreateDataRecordset dbOptiware98, SsQqLl, datApurosVales, dbOpenSnapshot

        SsQqLl = "SELECT * FROM qyMovCxApuros WHERE mcxControleCaixaId IN (SELECT ctrlcxId FROM ControleCaixa WHERE ctrlcxDataAbertura BetWeen #" & Format(dData1, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "# And #" & Format(dData2, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "#)"
        oUtils.CreateDataRecordset dbOptiware98, SsQqLl, datApurosMovimentos, dbOpenSnapshot

        ssqlMovCx = "Select Sum(xCredito)- Sum(xDebito) as xSaldo FROM qyMovCaixaCxSaldo WHERE mcxControleCaixaId IN (SELECT ctrlcxId FROM ControleCaixa WHERE ctrlcxDataAbertura BetWeen #" & Format(dData1, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "# And #" & Format(dData2, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "#)"

        SsQqLl = "SELECT SUM(valValor) as [xValor] FROM Qyvales WHERE ((valDataHoraPago) Is Not Null) AND valControleCaixaId IN (SELECT ctrlcxId FROM ControleCaixa WHERE ctrlcxDataAbertura BetWeen #" & Format(dData1, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "# And #" & Format(dData2, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "#)"
    End If

    ' Total de Vales
    oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, SsQqLl, xRs, dbOpenSnapshot
    With xRs
        TotVales = oUtils.Convert2Double(!xValor)
        .Close
    End With
    Set xRs = Nothing

    'Total de Movimentos de Caixa
    oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, ssqlMovCx, xRs, dbOpenSnapshot
    If xRs.RecordCount >= 0 Then
        lblApurosMov(0).Caption = Format$(xRs!xSaldo, "Standard")
    End If
    Set xRs = Nothing


    SsQqLl = "SELECT SUM(ctrlcxNumerario) AS [xNumero], SUM(ctrlcxCheques) AS [xCheques], " _
             & "SUM(ctrlcxMultiBanco) AS [xMB], SUM(ctrlcxCartaoCredito) AS [xCartaoC], " _
             & "SUM(ctrlcxNotaCredito) AS [xNC], SUM(ctrlcxTotalVendas) AS [xTotVendas], " _
             & "SUM(ctrlcxTotalDevolucoes) AS [xTotDev], SUM(ctrlcxTotalPagamentos) AS [xTotPagamento], " _
             & "SUM(ctrlcxTotalVales) AS [xTotVales], SUM(ctrlcxTotalCreditos) as [xTotCreditos], " _
             & "SUM(ctrlcxTotalReceber) AS [xTotCaixa], " _
             & "(SUM(ctrlcxTotalReceber) - SUM(ctrlcxTotalReceberInt)) as [xDifCx], " _
             & "SUM(ctrlcxPreDatados) as [xPreDatados], SUM(ctrlcxQtVendas) as [NVendas] " _
             & "FROM qyControleCxMovimentos " _
             & "Where ctrlcxDataAbertura >= #" & Format(dData1, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "# and ctrlcxDataAbertura <= #" & Format(dData2, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "#"

    If lidControleCaixa <> 0 Then
        SsQqLl = SsQqLl & " and ctrlcxCaixaId = " & lidControleCaixa
    End If

    With datApuroGeral.Recordset
        TotApuros = oUtils.Convert2Double(!cabapTotalValor) - oUtils.Convert2Double(!cabapTotalDesc)
    End With

    oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, SsQqLl, xRs, dbOpenSnapshot
    With xRs
        lblApurosMovCx(0).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!xNumero), "Standard")
        lblApurosMovCx(1).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!xCheques), "Standard")
        lblApurosMovCx(2).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!xPreDatados), "Standard")
        lblApurosMovCx(3).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!xMB), "Standard")
        lblApurosMovCx(4).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!xCartaoC), "Standard")
        lblApurosMovCx(5).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(TotVales), "Standard")
        lblApurosMovCx(6).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!xTotPagamento), "Standard")
        lblApurosMovCx(7).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!xTotDev), "Standard")
        lblApurosMovCx(8).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!xTotVales), "Standard")
        lblApurosMovCx(9).Caption = oUtils.Convert2Integer(!NVendas)
        lblApurosMovCx(10).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!xTotCaixa), "Standard")
        lblApurosMovCx(11).Caption = Format$(TotApuros, "Standard")
        lblApurosMovCx(12).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!xDifCx), "Standard")
        lblApurosMovCx(13).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!xNc), "Standard")
        .Close
    End With
    Set xRs = Nothing
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "CalculoMovimentosCx()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

'Calculos para o apuros de caixa, Carregamento do grid apuro de caixa
Private Sub CalculoApurosCaixa(Optional ByVal bRecal As Variant)

    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim rsApuros As Recordset, rsFam As Recordset
    Dim sSQL As String, sTipoApuro As String, sCaixa As String
    Dim sPeriodo As String, sFamilia As String
    Dim iRow As Integer, lIdCaixa As Long
    Dim byFirst As Byte, byteTipoApuro As Byte
    Dim xAux As Variant
    Dim dTTotal As Double
    Dim sSqlApuro As String
    Dim vField As Variant

    Screen.MousePointer = vbHourglass

    bRecal = IIf(IsMissing(bRecal), False, bRecal)
    If bRecal Then
        Dim iPos As Integer
        iPos = InStr(1, lblApurosCX(2), "ate")
        ReDim vPeriodo(1)
        vPeriodo(0) = Mid(lblApurosCX(2).Caption, 1, iPos - 1)
        vPeriodo(1) = Mid(lblApurosCX(2).Caption, iPos + 3)
    End If

    byteTipoApuro = cboApurosCX(0).ListIndex
    Set xaApurosCx = Nothing
    xaApurosCx.ReDim 0, -1, 0, NumColunasApurosCX
    tdgApurosCx.Array = xaApurosCx
    tdgApurosCx.ReBind

    If byteTipoApuro < 3 Then
        'Vendas (todas, facturadas, não facturadas)
        sSQL = "SELECT " & _
            "  IIF((NOT ISNULL(art.artID)), fam.famNome, IIF((NOT ISNULL(lo.loID)), ""Lentes Oftálmicas"", IIF(NOT ISNULL(lc.lcID), ""Lentes de Contacto"", ""Desconhecido""))) AS Familia, " & vbCrLf & _
            "  IIF((NOT ISNULL(art.artID)), fam.famID, IIF((NOT ISNULL(lo.loID)), -1, IIF(NOT ISNULL(lc.lcID), -2, 0))) AS FamiliaID, " & vbCrLf & _
            "  SUM(mov.movQt) AS Quantidade, " & vbCrLf & _
            "  SUM(mov.movPVP * mov.movQt) AS Valor, " & vbCrLf & _
            "  SUM(mov.movValorComp) AS Comparticipacao, " & vbCrLf & _
            "  SUM(mov.movDesconto) AS Desconto, " & vbCrLf & _
            "  SUM(mov.movValorIVA) AS IVA, " & vbCrLf & _
            "  SUM(mov.movPVP * mov.movQt - movValorComp - movDesconto) AS Total " & vbCrLf & vbCrLf

        sSQL = sSQL & _
            "FROM (((((((MovimentosArtigos mov " & vbCrLf & _
            "INNER JOIN CabecalhoVendas cv ON mov.movIDCabVendas = cv.cabvenID) " & vbCrLf & _
            "INNER JOIN Existencias ext ON mov.movIDExistencia = ext.extID) " & vbCrLf & _
            "LEFT JOIN Artigos art ON ext.extIDArtigo = art.artID) " & vbCrLf & _
            "LEFT JOIN LO ON ext.extIDLenteOftalmica = LO.loID) " & vbCrLf & _
            "LEFT JOIN LC ON ext.extIDLenteContacto = LC.lcID) " & vbCrLf & _
            "LEFT JOIN Familias fam ON art.artIDFamilia = fam.famID) " & vbCrLf & _
            "LEFT JOIN LOFornecedores lof ON LO.loRefFornecedor = lof.lofReferencia) " & vbCrLf & _
            "LEFT JOIN LCFornecedores lcf ON LC.lcRefFornecedor = lcf.lcfReferencia " & vbCrLf & vbCrLf
            
        sSQL = sSQL & "WHERE cv.CabVenEstado = 0 AND mov.movActivo = True "
        
        ' Filtro de Data
        sSQL = sSQL & _
            " AND cabVenData >= " & SqlDate(vPeriodo(0)) & _
            " AND cabvenData <= " & SqlDate(vPeriodo(1))
        
        ' Filtro de Tipo de Apuro
        Select Case byteTipoApuro
            Case 0 ' Vendas (Global)
                ' nada
            Case 1 ' Vendas Facturadas
                sSQL = sSQL & " AND cabvenIdCabDoc <> 0 "
            Case 2 ' Vendas Não Facturadas
                sSQL = sSQL & " AND cabvenIdCabDoc = 0 "
        End Select
        
        ' Filtro de Caixa
        If oUtils.Convert2Long(cboApurosCX(1).Tag) > 0 Then
           sSQL = sSQL & " AND cabVenIdCaixa = " & str(Int(cboApurosCX(1).Tag))
        End If
        
        sSQL = sSQL & vbCrLf & "GROUP BY " & _
            "IIF((NOT ISNULL(art.artID)), fam.famID, IIF((NOT ISNULL(lo.loID)), -1, IIF(NOT ISNULL(lc.lcID), -2, 0))), " & _
            "IIF((NOT ISNULL(art.artID)), fam.famNome, IIF((NOT ISNULL(lo.loID)), ""Lentes Oftálmicas"", IIF(NOT ISNULL(lc.lcID), ""Lentes de Contacto"", ""Desconhecido""))) "
            
        sSQL = sSQL & vbCrLf & "ORDER BY SUM(mov.movPVP * mov.movQt - movValorComp - movDesconto) DESC "
        
        Set rsApuros = dbo.OpenRecordset(sSQL, dbOpenForwardOnly)
        With rsApuros
            Do Until .EOF
                If !Quantidade > 0 Then
                    iRow = xaApurosCx.UpperBound(1) + 1
                    xaApurosCx.Insert 1, iRow

                    xaApurosCx.value(iRow, 0) = .fields("Familia").value
                    xaApurosCx.value(iRow, 1) = .fields("Quantidade").value
                    xaApurosCx.value(iRow, 2) = .fields("Valor").value
                    xaApurosCx.value(iRow, 3) = .fields("Desconto").value
                    xaApurosCx.value(iRow, 4) = .fields("Comparticipacao").value
                    xaApurosCx.value(iRow, 5) = .fields("Total").value
                    dTTotal = dTTotal + .fields("Total").value
                    xaApurosCx.value(iRow, 6) = .fields("IVA").value
                    
                    Select Case !Familia
                        Case "Lentes Oftálmicas", "Lentes de Contacto"
                            xaApurosCx.value(iRow, 8) = Familias_ObtemID(!Familia)
                        Case Else
                            xaApurosCx.value(iRow, 8) = .fields("FamiliaID").value
                    End Select
                End If
                .MoveNext
            Loop
            .Close
        End With
    
    Else    'Facturas

        sCaixa = IIf(oUtils.Convert2Long(cboApurosCX(1).Tag) = 0, "<> 0", "= " & oUtils.Convert2Long(cboApurosCX(1).Tag))
        sSQL = "SELECT LinhasDocumentos.LinDocIdFamilia AS FamiliaID, " & _
               "Familias.famNome AS FamiliaNome, " & _
               "Sum(([LinDocQt]*[lindocpvp])) AS Valor, " & _
               "Sum(LinhasDocumentos.LinDocQt) AS Quantidade, " & _
               "Sum(LinhasDocumentos.LinDocDesconto) AS Desconto, " & _
               "Sum(LinhasDocumentos.LinDocComp) AS Comparticipacao, " & _
               "Sum(([LinDocQt]*[lindocpvp]-[lindocDesconto])) AS Total, " & _
               "Sum(LinhasDocumentos.LinDocValorIva) AS ValorIva " & _
               "FROM Familias INNER JOIN (CabecalhoDocumentos INNER JOIN LinhasDocumentos ON " & _
               "CabecalhoDocumentos.CabDocId = LinhasDocumentos.LinDocIdCabDoc) ON " & _
               "Familias.famId = LinhasDocumentos.LinDocIdFamilia " & _
               "WHERE CabecalhoDocumentos.CabDocIdCaixa " & sCaixa & " AND " & _
               "CabecalhoDocumentos.CabDocData >= #" & Format$(vPeriodo(0), "mm-dd-yyyy") & "# AND " & _
               "CabecalhoDocumentos.CabDocData <= #" & Format$(vPeriodo(1), "mm-dd-yyyy") & "# AND " & _
               "CabecalhoDocumentos.CabDocEstado = 0 AND " & _
               "(CabecalhoDocumentos.CabDocTipoDoc = 1 OR CabecalhoDocumentos.CabDocTipoDoc = 2) " & _
               "GROUP BY LinhasDocumentos.LinDocIdFamilia, Familias.famNome " & _
               "ORDER BY Familias.famNome;"
        Set rsApuros = dbo.OpenRecordset(sSQL, dbOpenSnapshot)
        With rsApuros
            If (.RecordCount > 0) Then
                dTTotal = 0
                Do While Not .EOF
                    iRow = xaApurosCx.UpperBound(1) + 1
                    xaApurosCx.Insert 1, iRow
                    vField = !FamiliaNome: xaApurosCx(iRow, 0) = vField
                    vField = !Quantidade: xaApurosCx(iRow, 1) = vField
                    vField = !valor: xaApurosCx(iRow, 2) = vField
                    vField = !Desconto: xaApurosCx(iRow, 3) = vField
                    vField = !Comparticipacao: xaApurosCx(iRow, 4) = vField
                    vField = !Total: xaApurosCx(iRow, 5) = vField
                    vField = !ValorIVA: xaApurosCx(iRow, 6) = vField
                    vField = !FamiliaID: xaApurosCx(iRow, 8) = vField
                    dTTotal = dTTotal + !Total
                    .MoveNext
                Loop
                .Close
            End If
        End With

    End If


    CalculoPesoApuro dTTotal

    tdgApurosCx.ReBind
    Screen.MousePointer = vbDefault
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "CalculoApurosCaixa()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

'Calculo do Peso dos apuros
Private Sub CalculoPesoApuro(ByVal dTTotal As Double)
    Dim iNFam As Integer
    Dim lQt As Long
    Dim dTValor As Double, dTDesc As Double
    Dim dTComp As Double, dTIVA As Double
    Dim iRow As Integer
    Dim iErro As Integer
    On Error GoTo erro
    With xaApurosCx
        For iRow = 0 To .UpperBound(1)
            If .value(iRow, 1) <> 0 Then
                iNFam = iNFam + 1
                lQt = lQt + .value(iRow, 1)
                dTValor = dTValor + .value(iRow, 2)
                dTDesc = dTDesc + .value(iRow, 3)
                dTComp = dTComp + .value(iRow, 4)
                dTIVA = dTIVA + .value(iRow, 6)
                If dTTotal <> 0 Then
                    .value(iRow, 7) = .value(iRow, 5) * 100 / dTTotal
                End If
            End If
        Next iRow
        .Insert 1, iRow
        .Insert 1, iRow + 1
        iRow = iRow + 1
        .value(iRow, 0) = iNFam
        .value(iRow, 1) = lQt
        .value(iRow, 2) = dTValor
        .value(iRow, 3) = dTDesc
        .value(iRow, 4) = dTComp
        .value(iRow, 5) = dTTotal
        .value(iRow, 6) = dTIVA
        .value(iRow, 7) = 100
    End With
    With tabApuros
        .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(0), lQt <> 0
        .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(1), lQt <> 0
        .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(2), lQt <> 0
    End With
    cboApurosCX(1).Enabled = lQt <> 0
    cboApurosCX(0).Enabled = lQt <> 0
    cmdApurosCx(5).Enabled = lQt <> 0
    cmdApurosCx(4).Enabled = lQt <> 0
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "CalculoPesoApuro()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub
'----------------------------------------------------------------
' Fim das funcoes de apuro de caixa
'----------------------------------------------------------------

'Reabertura de caixa
Private Sub ReaberturaCaixa()

    Dim lidControleCaixa As Long
    Dim rs As Recordset
    Dim dDataCx As Date
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim rsArmazens As Recordset
    Dim vLastExport As Variant

    On Error GoTo erro

    Set rsArmazens = dbo.OpenRecordset("Armazens", dbOpenTable)
    With rsArmazens
        Do While Not .EOF
            If IsDate(!armEFim) Then
                If IsDate(vLastExport) Then
                    If (!armEFim > CDate(vLastExport)) Then
                        vLastExport = !armEFim
                    End If
                Else
                    vLastExport = !armEFim
                End If
            End If
            .MoveNext
        Loop
    End With
    Set rsArmazens = Nothing

    lidControleCaixa = oUtils.Convert2Long(tabCaixa.Tag)
    oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, "ControleCaixa", rs, dbOpenDynaset
    With rs
        .FindFirst " ctrlcxId = " & lidControleCaixa
        If .NoMatch Then
            MsgBox "O controle de caixa não existe!", vbInformation
            rs.Close
            Set rs = Nothing
            Exit Sub
        End If
        If IsDate(vLastExport) Then
            If (CDate(vLastExport) > Now) Then
                MsgBox "Não é possível reabrir uma caixa com a data anterior à da última consolidação!", vbInformation, msgInformation
                Exit Sub
            End If
        End If
        .edit
        !ctrlcxNumerarioInt = 0
        !ctrlcxChequesInt = 0
        !ctrlcxPreDatadosInt = 0
        !ctrlcxMultibancoInt = 0
        !ctrlcxCartaoCreditoInt = 0
        !ctrlcxNotaCreditoInt = 0
        !ctrlcxTotalValesInt = 0
        !ctrlcxTotalPagamentosInt = 0
        !ctrlcxTotalDevolucoesInt = 0
        !ctrlcxTotalReceberInt = 0
        !ctrlcxDataFecho = Null
        !ctrlcxOperadorFechId = 0
        !ctrlcxObsFecho = ""
        !ctrlcxTrocosProxCx = 0
        !ctrlcxHoraFecho = Null
        dDataCx = !ctrlcxDataAbertura
        RsUpdate rs
    End With
    rs.Close
    Set rs = Nothing

    dbo.Execute "Update Depositos Set depCreator = '" & aUser(C_UserLogin) & "', depModified = #" & Now & "#, depActivo = False Where depIdCtrlCx = " & lidControleCaixa

    tabCaixa.TabSetChildEnabled cmdCxDiaria(3), True
    tabCaixa.TabSetChildEnabled cmdCxDiaria(2), False
    tabCaixa.TabSetChildEnabled cmdCxDiaria(0), False
    tabCaixa.TabSetChildEnabled cmdCxDiaria(1), False
    picCxDiaria(1).Enabled = True
    picCxDiaria(0).Enabled = True
    txtCxDiaria(1).SetFocus
    lblCx(1).Caption = "Aberta"
    lblCx(1).BackColor = ColorCXAberta

    'datCaixa.Recordset.Requery

    If dDataCx = Date Then
        With tabPos
            .Tab = TABPosAtendimento
            .TabState = IIf(NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_ATEND"), TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT, TAB_STATE_ENABLED)
            .Tab = TABPosCreditos
            .TabState = IIf(NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_VALORESPAG"), TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT, TAB_STATE_ENABLED)
            .Tab = TABPosDocumentos
            .TabState = IIf(NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_DOC"), TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT, TAB_STATE_ENABLED)
        End With
    End If
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ReaberturaCaixa()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

'Fecho da caixa do dia
Private Sub FechoCaixa()
    Dim lidControleCaixa As Long
    Dim rs As Recordset
    Dim dDataCx As Date
    Dim sAuxiliar As String
    Dim IdArray(2) As Long    ' 0 Id Num, 1 Id Mb, 2 Id CC
    Dim ValorArray(2) As Double    ' 0 Valor Num, 1 Valor Mb, 2 Valor CC
    Dim rr As Byte
    Dim iErro As Integer, sMensagem As String
    Dim fTransaction As Boolean

    Dim sSQL As String
    Dim rsUsers As Recordset

    On Error GoTo erro
    
    lidControleCaixa = oUtils.Convert2Long(tabCaixa.Tag)

    sSQL = "SELECT * FROM qryUtilizadoresCaixa WHERE ControleCaixaID = " & lidControleCaixa & " AND " & _
           "UserID <> " & aUser(C_UserId)
    Set rsUsers = dbo.OpenRecordset(sSQL, dbOpenSnapshot)
    With rsUsers
        If (.RecordCount > 0) Then
            MsgBox "Não é possível realizar o Fecho de Caixa neste momento!" & vbCrLf & _
                   "Existem outros utilizadores no Optiware a trabalhar com esta Caixa.", vbInformation, msgInformation
            Set rsUsers = Nothing
            GoTo Abortar
        End If
        .Close
    End With
    Set rsUsers = Nothing
    
    If MsgBox("Confirma o fecho da caixa?", vbOKCancel + vbQuestion, "Fechar Caixa") <> vbOK Then
        Exit Sub
    End If

    OptiwareEx.BeginTrans "frmPosMain.FechoCaixa"
    fTransaction = True
    
    ' Obtém identificadores de tipos de movimento de depósito
    sAuxiliar = " tpCodigo = 'DEP.NUM'"
    oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, "Select tpCodigo, tpId from TipoMovimento", rs, dbOpenSnapshot
    With rs
        For rr = 0 To 2
            If rr = 2 Then sAuxiliar = "tpCodigo = 'DEP.CC'"
            .FindFirst sAuxiliar
            If Not .NoMatch Then IdArray(rr) = !tpId
            sAuxiliar = "tpCodigo = 'DEP.MB'"
        Next rr
    End With
    rs.Close
    Set rs = Nothing
    
    ' Fecha a caixa
    Set rs = dbo.OpenRecordset("SELECT * FROM ControleCaixa WHERE ctrlcxId = " & str(lidControleCaixa), dbOpenDynaset)
    With rs
        If .EOF Then
            rs.Close
            Err.Raise Erro_NaoEncontrado, "FechoCaixa", "O controle de caixa não foi encontrado."
        End If
        
        If Not IsNull(!ctrlcxDataFecho) Then
            rs.Close
            sMensagem = "A caixa já foi fechada."
            GoTo Abortar
        End If
        
        ' Verifica que não houve alterações entretanto.
        If (Round(!ctrlcxNumerario, 2) <> oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(1).Caption)) Or _
            (Round(!ctrlcxCheques, 2) <> oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(2).Caption)) Or _
            (Round(!ctrlcxPreDatados, 2) <> oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(3).Caption)) Or _
            (Round(!ctrlcxMultibanco, 2) <> oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(4).Caption)) Or _
            (Round(!ctrlcxCartaoCredito, 2) <> oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(5).Caption)) Or _
            (Round(!ctrlcxNotaCredito, 2) <> oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(6).Caption)) Then
            rs.Close
            sMensagem = "Os valores de caixa foram alterados desde o início da conferência. Por favor reconfirme."
            GoTo Abortar
        End If
        
        ValorArray(0) = oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxNumerario)
        ValorArray(1) = oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxMultibanco)
        ValorArray(2) = oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxCartaoCredito)

        sAuxiliar = Caixa_ObtemNome(!ctrlcxCaixaid)
        .edit
        !ctrlcxmoeda = aEuro(C_TipoMoeda)
        !ctrlcxTaxaCV = aEuro(C_TaxaEuro)
        !ctrlcxQtVendas = oUtils.Convert2Long(lblCxValores(0).Caption)
        !ctrlcxNumerarioInt = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(1).Text)
        !ctrlcxChequesInt = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(2).Text)
        !ctrlcxPreDatadosInt = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(3).Text)
        !ctrlcxMultibancoInt = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(4).Text)
        !ctrlcxCartaoCreditoInt = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(5).Text)
        !ctrlcxNotaCreditoInt = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(6).Text)
        !ctrlcxTotalValesInt = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(7).Text)
        !ctrlcxTotalPagamentosInt = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(8).Text)
        !ctrlcxTotalDevolucoesInt = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(9).Text)
        !ctrlcxTotalReceberInt = oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(21).Caption)
        !ctrlcxDataFecho = Date
        !ctrlcxOperadorFechId = aUser(C_UserId)
        !ctrlcxTrocosProxCx = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(10).Text)
        !ctrlcxHoraFecho = Time
        dDataCx = !ctrlcxDataAbertura
        RsUpdate rs
    End With
    rs.Close
    Set rs = Nothing
    
    oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, "Depositos", rs, dbOpenDynaset
    With rs
        For rr = 0 To 2
            If ValorArray(rr) <> 0 Then
                .AddNew
                !depCreator = aUser(C_UserLogin)
                !depModified = Now
                !depIDtipo = IdArray(rr)
                !depData = Date
                !depValor = ValorArray(rr)
                !depCaixa = sAuxiliar
                !depdescricao = "Fecho CX:" & sAuxiliar & " - " & Date
                !depIdCtrlCx = lidControleCaixa
                !depMoeda = aEuro(C_TipoMoeda)
                !depTaxaCV = aEuro(C_TaxaEuro)
                RsUpdate rs
            End If
        Next rr
    End With
    rs.Close
    Set rs = Nothing

    OptiwareEx.CommitTrans
    fTransaction = False

    ' Recarrega
    Carrega_CaixadoDia

    ' Envia SMS
    Dim rscontacto As Recordset
    Set rscontacto = dbo.OpenRecordset("SELECT cfgContacto FROM ConfiguracoesSMS", dbOpenDynaset)
    If rscontacto.RecordCount > 0 Then
        If IsEmpty(rscontacto!cfgContacto) Or rscontacto!cfgContacto = "" Or IsNull(rscontacto!cfgContacto) Or Not ValidarNumeroTlm(rscontacto!cfgContacto & vbNullString) Then
            Exit Sub
        End If
        
        Dim Contacto As String
        Contacto = "Contactar de volta"
        
        Dim tipo As String
        VerificarRede Left$(rscontacto!cfgContacto, 2), tipo, Contacto
        If tipo = "Cartão" Then
            Dim erro As Long
            erro = 0
            EnviarSMS "A caixa da loja " & aLoja(C_NomeLoja) & " foi encerrada com o total de caixa de " & lblCxValores(10).Caption & " euros", Contacto, erro, False
        Else
            EnviarSMSGateway Contacto, "A caixa da loja " & aLoja(C_NomeLoja) & " foi encerrada com o total de " & lblCxValores(10).Caption & " euros", False, False
        End If
    End If
    
    Exit Sub
erro:
    ErrorHandle "frmPosMain", "FechoCaixa()"

Abortar:
    On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    If fTransaction Then OptiwareEx.RollbackTrans
    
    If sMensagem <> "" Then
        MsgBox sMensagem, vbExclamation, "Fechar Caixa"
    End If
    
    Carrega_CaixadoDia
End Sub



'Carrega o Resume de caixa
Private Sub Carrega_CaixadoDia()
    Dim rs As Recordset
    Dim lNumVendas As Long, lidControleCaixa As Long
    Dim xData As Date
    Dim dArray(9) As Double
    Dim dArrayInt(8) As Double, dSoma As Double
    Dim byteRR As Byte
    Dim iErro As Integer

    ' Nova Variáveis
    Dim dSomaAppIn As Double    ' Soma dos valores de entrada em Caixa da Aplicação
    Dim dSomaAppOut As Double    ' Soma dos valores de saida de Caixa da Aplicação
    Dim dSomaUsrIn As Double    ' Soma dos valores de entrada em Caixa do Utilizador
    Dim dSomaUsrOut As Double    ' Soma dos valores de saida de Caixa do Utilizador

    On Error GoTo erro
    lidControleCaixa = oUtils.Convert2Long(tabCaixa.Tag)    'Id do Controle de caixa
    With datCaixa.Recordset
        .FindFirst " ctrlcxId = " & lidControleCaixa
        If .NoMatch Then
            MsgBox "A caixa indicada não existe!", vbInformation
            bAbortar = True
            Exit Sub
        End If

        xData = !ctrlcxDataAbertura

        oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, "SELECT COUNT(*) AS Count FROM CabecalhoVendas WHERE cabvenIdCaixa = " & !ctrlcxCaixaid & " and cabVenData = " & SqlDate(xData), rs, dbOpenForwardOnly
        With rs
            If Not .EOF Then
                lNumVendas = CLng(rs!Count)
            End If
            .Close
        End With
        
        m_CaixaFM = Caixa_ObtemFundoManeio(!ctrlcxCaixaid)
        If m_CaixaFM > 0 Then lblCxDiaria(23).Caption = "Fundo Maneio"

        ' Valores da Aplicação
        ' Entradas em Caixa
        lblCxValores(1).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxNumerario, "Standard")  ' Numerário
        lblCxValores(2).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxCheques, "Standard")  ' Cheques
        lblCxValores(3).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxPreDatados, "Standard")  ' Pre datados
        lblCxValores(4).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxMultibanco, "Standard")   ' Multibanco
        lblCxValores(5).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxCartaoCredito, "Standard")   ' Cartões de Crédito
        lblCxValores(6).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxNotaCredito, "Standard")  ' Pag. por Nota de Crédito
        lblCxValores(23).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxTotalValesPag, "Standard")  ' Pag. de Vales de Caixa
        lblCxValores(24).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxTransferencias, "Standard")    ' Pag. de Vales de Caixa
        lblCxValores(25).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxTransferencias, "Standard")    ' Pag. de Vales de Caixa
        ' Saidas de Caixa
        lblCxValores(7).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxTotalVales, "Standard")  ' Vales de Caixa emitidos
        lblCxValores(8).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxTotalPagamentos, "Standard")  ' Pagamentos de Caixa
        lblCxValores(9).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxTotalDevolucoes, "Standard")  ' Notas de Crédito Emitidas

        ' Valores do Utilizador
        ' Entradas em Caixa
        txtCxDiaria(1).Text = Format$(!ctrlcxNumerarioInt, "Standard")  ' Numerário
        txtCxDiaria(2).Text = Format$(!ctrlcxChequesInt, "Standard")    ' Cheques
        txtCxDiaria(3).Text = Format$(!ctrlcxPreDatadosInt, "Standard")    ' Pre datados
        txtCxDiaria(4).Text = Format$(!ctrlcxMultibancoInt, "Standard")    ' Multibanco
        txtCxDiaria(5).Text = Format$(!ctrlcxCartaoCreditoInt, "Standard")    ' Cartões de Crédito
        txtCxDiaria(6).Text = Format$(!ctrlcxNotaCreditoInt, "Standard")    ' Pag. por Nota de Crédito
        ' Saidas de Caixa
        txtCxDiaria(7).Text = Format$(!ctrlcxTotalValesInt, "Standard")    ' Vales de Caixa emitidos
        txtCxDiaria(8).Text = Format$(!ctrlcxTotalPagamentosInt, "Standard")    ' Pagamentos de Caixa
        txtCxDiaria(9).Text = Format$(!ctrlcxTotalDevolucoesInt, "Standard")    ' Notas de Crédito Emitidas



        dSomaAppIn = !ctrlcxNumerario + !ctrlcxCheques + _
                     !ctrlcxPreDatados + !ctrlcxMultibanco + _
                     !ctrlcxCartaoCredito + !ctrlcxNotaCredito '+ _
                     '!ctrlcxTotalValesPag
                     
        If Config_GetRemoverNotasCreditoTotalCaixa Then
            dSomaAppIn = dSomaAppIn - !ctrlcxNotaCredito
        End If
        
        If Config_Caixa_SubtraiDevolucoes Then
            dSomaAppOut = !ctrlcxTotalVales + !ctrlcxTotalPagamentos + !ctrlcxTotalDevolucoes
        End If


        dSomaUsrIn = !ctrlcxNumerarioInt + !ctrlcxChequesInt + _
                     !ctrlcxPreDatadosInt + !ctrlcxMultibancoInt + _
                     !ctrlcxCartaoCreditoInt + !ctrlcxNotaCreditoInt
                     
        If Config_GetRemoverNotasCreditoTotalCaixa Then
            dSomaUsrIn = dSomaUsrIn - !ctrlcxNotaCredito
        End If

        If Config_Caixa_SubtraiDevolucoes Then
            dSomaUsrOut = !ctrlcxTotalValesInt + !ctrlcxTotalPagamentosInt + !ctrlcxTotalDevolucoesInt
        Else
            dSomaUsrOut = 0
        End If

        If Not IsNull(!ctrlcxDataFecho) Then    ' Caixa Fechada

            '            For byteRR = 1 To 9
            '                txtCxDiaria(byteRR).Text = Format$(dArrayInt(byteRR - 1), "Standard")
            '                dSoma = dSoma + oUtils.Convert2Double(dArrayInt(byteRR - 1))
            '            Next byteRR
        Else                                    ' Caixa Aberta
            For byteRR = 1 To 10
                txtCxDiaria(byteRR).Text = Format$(0, "Standard")
            Next byteRR
            dSoma = 0
        End If
        
        

        ' Diferença de Valores
        ' Entradas em Caixa
        lblCxValores(11).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxNumerarioInt - Abs(IIf(!ctrlcxNumerario > 0, !ctrlcxNumerario, 0)) + m_CaixaFM, "Standard")   ' Numerário
        lblCxValores(12).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxChequesInt - Abs(!ctrlcxCheques), "Standard")  ' Cheques
        lblCxValores(13).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxPreDatadosInt - Abs(!ctrlcxPreDatados), "Standard")    ' Pre datados
        lblCxValores(14).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxMultibancoInt - Abs(!ctrlcxMultibanco), "Standard")  ' Multibanco
        lblCxValores(15).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxCartaoCreditoInt - Abs(!ctrlcxCartaoCredito), "Standard")   ' Cartões de Crédito
        lblCxValores(16).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxNotaCreditoInt - Abs(!ctrlcxNotaCredito), "Standard")    ' Pag. por Nota de Crédito
        ' Saidas de Caixa
        lblCxValores(17).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxTotalValesInt - Abs(!ctrlcxTotalVales), "Standard")    ' Vales de Caixa emitidos
        lblCxValores(18).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxTotalPagamentosInt - Abs(!ctrlcxTotalPagamentos), "Standard")    ' Pagamentos de Caixa
        lblCxValores(19).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxTotalDevolucoesInt - Abs(!ctrlcxTotalDevolucoes), "Standard")    ' Notas de Crédito Emitidas

        '        lblCxValores(11).Tag = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxNumerarioInt) - oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxNumerario), "Standard")  ' Numerário
        '        lblCxValores(12).Tag = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxChequesInt) - oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxCheques), "Standard")  ' Cheques
        '        lblCxValores(13).Tag = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxPreDatadosInt) - oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxPreDatados), "Standard") ' Pre datados
        '        lblCxValores(14).Tag = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxMultibancoInt) - oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxMultibanco), "Standard")  ' Multibanco
        '        lblCxValores(15).Tag = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxCartaoCreditoInt) - oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxCartaoCredito), "Standard")   ' Cartões de Crédito
        '        lblCxValores(16).Tag = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxNotaCreditoInt) - oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxNotaCredito), "Standard") ' Pag. por Nota de Crédito
        ' Saidas de Caixa
        '        lblCxValores(17).Tag = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxTotalValesInt) - oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxTotalVales), "Standard") ' Vales de Caixa emitidos
        '        lblCxValores(18).Tag = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxTotalPagamentosint) - oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxTotalPagamentos), "Standard") ' Pagamentos de Caixa
        '        lblCxValores(19).Tag = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxTotalDevolucoesInt) - oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxTotalDevolucoes), "Standard") ' Notas de Crédito Emitidas

        'lblCxValores(11).Tag = oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxNumerario)  ' Numerário
        'lblCxValores(12).Tag = oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxCheques)  ' Cheques
        'lblCxValores(13).Tag = oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxPreDatados)  ' Pre datados
        'lblCxValores(14).Tag = oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxMultibanco)   ' Multibanco
        'lblCxValores(15).Tag = oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxCartaoCredito)   ' Cartões de Crédito
        'lblCxValores(16).Tag = oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxNotaCredito)  ' Pag. por Nota de Crédito
        ' Saidas de Caixa
        'lblCxValores(17).Tag = oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxTotalVales)  ' Vales de Caixa emitidos
        'lblCxValores(18).Tag = oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxTotalPagamentos)  ' Pagamentos de Caixa
        'lblCxValores(19).Tag = oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxTotalDevolucoes)  ' Notas de Crédito Emitidas

        '        For byteRR = 0 To 8
        '            lblCxValores(byteRR + 1).Caption = Format$(dArray(byteRR), "Standard")
        '            With lblCxValores(byteRR + 11)
        '                .Caption = Format$(dArrayInt(byteRR) - dArray(byteRR), "Standard")
        '                .Tag = Format$(-dArray(byteRR), "Standard")
        '            End With
        '        Next byteRR

        lblCxValores(0).Caption = lNumVendas

        '        lblCxValores(10).Caption = Format$(dArray(9), "Standard")

        lblCxValores(10).Caption = Format$(dSomaAppIn - Abs(dSomaAppOut), "Standard")    '+ IIf(IsNull(!ctrlcxTransferencias), 0, !ctrlcxTransferencias)

        '        With lblCxValores(20)
        '            .Caption = Format$(dSoma - dArray(9), "Standard")
        '            .Tag = Format$(-dArray(9), "Standard")
        '        End With
        '        lblCxValores(21).Caption = Format$(dSoma, "Standard")
        lblCxValores(20).Caption = Format$((dSomaUsrIn - Abs(dSomaUsrOut) - Abs(dSomaAppIn - m_CaixaFM - Abs(dSomaAppOut))), "Standard")
        '        lblCxValores(20).Tag = Format$(-(dSomaAppIn - dSomaAppOut) - (dSomaUsrIn - dSomaUsrOut), "Standard")
        lblCxValores(21).Caption = Format$(dSomaUsrIn - Abs(dSomaUsrOut), "Standard")
        '        lblCxValores(21).Tag = Format$(dSomaUsrIn - dSomaUsrOut, "Standard")
        lblCxValores(22).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxValorAbertura, "Standard")
        lblCxValores(23).Caption = Format$(!ctrlcxTotalValesPag, "Standard")
        lblCx(0).Caption = !ctrlcxDataAbertura
        If IsNull(!ctrlcxDataFecho) Then
            lblCx(1).Caption = "Aberta"
            lblCx(1).BackColor = ColorCXAberta
        Else
            lblCx(1).Caption = "Fechada"
            lblCx(1).BackColor = ColorCXFechada
        End If
        txtCxDiaria(10).Text = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(!ctrlcxTrocosProxCx), "Standard")

        tabCaixa.TabSetChildEnabled cmdCxDiaria(3), IsNull(!ctrlcxDataFecho)
        tabCaixa.TabSetChildEnabled cmdCxDiaria(2), Not IsNull(!ctrlcxDataFecho)
        tabCaixa.TabSetChildEnabled cmdCxDiaria(0), Not IsNull(!ctrlcxDataFecho)
        tabCaixa.TabSetChildEnabled cmdCxDiaria(1), Not IsNull(!ctrlcxDataFecho)
        picCxDiaria(0).Enabled = IsNull(!ctrlcxDataFecho)
        tabCaixa.TabSetChildEnabled picCxDiaria(1), IsNull(!ctrlcxDataFecho)

    End With
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "Carrega_CaixadoDia()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:      On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

'Chama o processar/consulta de uma venda
Public Sub StartfrmConsultaVenda(ByVal bVisible As Boolean, ByVal iPos As Integer, ByVal stipovenda As String, ByVal lidvendas As Long, ByVal lidcreditos As Long, Optional PagDirecto As Boolean = False)

    Dim iErro As Integer

    On Error GoTo erro

'    If Not PagDirecto Then
'        With datCreditos.Recordset
'            .edit
'            !cdIDUserMarcou = 0
'            .Update
'        End With
'    End If
    
    
' Mostra a form
    With frmPosConsultaVenda
        .lIdCredito = lidcreditos
        .PagamentoDirecto = PagDirecto
    
        Select Case stipovenda
            Case "Venda Rapida"
                .byteTipoVenda = VendasRapidas
                .Caption = "Pagamento de um Crédito (Venda Rápida)"
                .lblPosAtende(11).Caption = "Sub-Total"
                
                tdgCreditos.Columns("cdMarcar") = 0
                
            Case "Reparacao"
                .byteTipoVenda = CrdReparacoes
                .Caption = "Pagamento de um Crédito (Reparação)"
                .lblPosAtende(11).Caption = "Sub-Total"
        
            Case "Optometria"
                .byteTipoVenda = CrdObraOptometria
                .Caption = "Pagamento de um Crédito (Optometria)"
                .lblPosAtende(11).Caption = "Total da Obra"
        
            Case "Contactologia"
                .byteTipoVenda = CrdObraContactologia
                .Caption = "Pagamento de um Crédito (Contactologia)"
                .lblPosAtende(11).Caption = "Total da Obra"
                
            Case Else
                Err.Raise ERRO_UNKNOWN, "StartfrmConsultaVenda", "O tipo de venda " & stipovenda & " não é suportado."
        End Select
        
        .cmdVenda(0).Visible = bVisible
        .cmdVenda(1).Left = iPos
        .Show vbModal
    End With

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "StartfrmConsultaVenda()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

'Valida se a referencia no grid esta limpa
Private Function ReferenciaNotEmpty(ByRef lRow As Long) As Boolean
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim lRr As Long
    On Error GoTo erro
    ReferenciaNotEmpty = True
    With xaVendas
        For lRr = .LowerBound(1) To .UpperBound(1)
            If Trim(.value(lRr, 0)) = "" Then
                ReferenciaNotEmpty = False
                lRow = lRr
                Exit Function
            End If
        Next lRr
    End With

    Exit Function
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "ReferenciaNotEmpty()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Function

'inicializa a Venda Rapida
Private Sub LimpaVenda(bNomeSetFocus As Boolean)
    Debug_EscreveLinha "frmPosMain.LimpaVenda"

    Dim objText As TextBox
    Dim objCMD As CommandButton
    Dim lLastNumber As Long
    Dim objChk As CheckBox
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim myRs As Recordset
    On Error GoTo erro
    For Each objText In txtVenda
        objText.Text = ""
    Next
    
    edValores.Limpa
    
    lblTotais(0).Caption = ""
    lblTotais(1).Caption = ""
    lblTotais(2).Caption = ""
    lblTroco.Caption = ""

'    cboVenda(1).Text = cboVenda(1).List(0)
    dbcVenda(2).Text = ""
    lLastNumber = 1
    lIdCliente = 0

    'oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, "Contadores", myRs, dbOpenTable, dbDenyWrite + dbDenyRead, dbPessimistic
    lLastNumber = oUtils.Convert2Long(rsContadores!conNumeroVenda) + 1
    'myRs.Close
    'Set myRs = Nothing
    txtVenda(0).Text = lLastNumber
    If bNomeSetFocus Then
        'txtVenda(1).SetFocus
        Set xaVendas = Nothing
        xaVendas.ReDim 0, 0, 0, NumColunasVendasRapidas
        With tdgVenda
            .Array = xaVendas
            .Row = 0
            .ReBind
        End With
    End If
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "LimpaVenda()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    Screen.MousePointer = vbDefault
End Sub

Private Sub cboApuroGeral_Click(Index As Integer)
    If Index = 0 Then
        If cboApuroGeral(Index).ListIndex > 0 Then
            chkApuroGeral(1).Enabled = True
        Else
            chkApuroGeral(1).Enabled = False
            chkApuroGeral(1).value = 0
        End If
    End If
End Sub

Private Sub cboApuroGeral_KeyPress(Index As Integer, KeyAscii As Integer)
    If KeyAscii = 13 Then Sendkeys "{TAB}"
End Sub

Private Sub cboApurosCX_Click(Index As Integer)
    If Index = 1 Then
        Dim rs As Recordset

        oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, "qyCaixas", rs, dbOpenSnapshot
        With rs
            .FindFirst " cxNome = '" & cboApurosCX(1).Text & "'"
            cboApurosCX(1).Tag = IIf(.NoMatch, 0, !cxID)
        End With
        rs.Close
        Set rs = Nothing

    End If
End Sub

Private Sub cboApurosCX_KeyPress(Index As Integer, KeyAscii As Integer)
    If KeyAscii = 13 Then Sendkeys "{TAB}"
End Sub

End Sub

    Select Case Index

            optComparticipacao(1).Visible = (cboCxVendasGeral(0).ListIndex = 2)
    End Select

End Sub

Private Sub cboDoc_Click(Index As Integer)
    Dim strCbo As String
    Dim iErro As Integer
    On Error GoTo erro
    picTipoComparticipacao.Visible = True
    Select Case Index
        Case 0
            If GetSetting(TipoComparticipacao) Then
                picTipoComparticipacao.Visible = (cboDoc(0).ListIndex = 0)
            End If
        Case 1
            With chkDoc(0)
                If cboDoc(1).ListIndex > 0 Then
                    .Enabled = True
                Else
                    .value = 0
                    .Enabled = False
                End If
            End With
        Case 2
            With cboDoc(Index)
                If oUtils.Convert2Long(.Tag) <> .ListIndex Then txtDoc(0).Text = ""
                strCbo = Trim(.Text)
                .Tag = .ListIndex
                txtDoc(0).Visible = (.ListIndex <> 0)
                txtDoc(1).Visible = False
                chkDoc(1).Enabled = False

                cboDocCaixas.Visible = False    ' O Templo
                '            With cboDoc(Index)
                '                If oUtils.Convert2Long(.Tag) <> .ListIndex Then txtDoc(0).Text = ""
                '                strCbo = Trim(.Text)
                '                .Tag = .ListIndex
                '                txtDoc(0).Visible = (.ListIndex <> 0)
                '                txtDoc(1).Visible = False
                '                chkDoc(1).Enabled = False
                Select Case .ListIndex
                    Case 1    ' Numero doc
                        txtDoc(0).Width = 1400
                        txtDoc(0).MaxLength = 20

                        txtDoc(1).Visible = True
                        txtDoc(1).MaxLength = 20

                        chkDoc(1).value = 0
                        chkDoc(1).Enabled = True

                    Case 2    ' Numero NIF
                        txtDoc(0).Width = 1320
                        txtDoc(0).MaxLength = 10

                    Case 3    ' Nome
                        txtDoc(0).Width = 3060
                        txtDoc(0).MaxLength = 100

                    Case 4    ' Datas
                        txtDoc(0).Width = 3060
                        txtDoc(0).Enabled = False
                        txtDoc(0).MaxLength = 40
                        
                    Case 5
                        Dim rsCaixas As Recordset
                        cboDocCaixas.Clear
                        cboDocCaixas.AddItem "<Nenhuma>"
                        cboDocCaixas.ItemData(cboDocCaixas.NewIndex) = 0
                        Set rsCaixas = dbo.OpenRecordset("qyCaixas", dbOpenSnapshot)
                        With rsCaixas
                            Do While Not .EOF
                                cboDocCaixas.AddItem !cxNome
                                cboDocCaixas.ItemData(cboDocCaixas.NewIndex) = !cxID
                                .MoveNext
                            Loop
                        End With
                        Set rsCaixas = Nothing
                        cboDocCaixas.ListIndex = 0

                        txtDoc(0).Visible = True
                        txtDoc(1).Visible = False
                        cboDocCaixas.Visible = True    ' O Templo
                        chkDoc(1).Enabled = True
                        chkDoc(1).value = 0
                        strCbo = "Datas"
                        picTipoComparticipacao.Visible = False
                        
                    Case 6
                        txtDoc(0).Width = 3060
                        txtDoc(0).MaxLength = 100
                        
                    Case 7 ' serie
                        txtDoc(0).Width = 1320
                        txtDoc(0).MaxLength = 10
                End Select
            End With
            cmdDoc(6).Enabled = (strCbo = "Datas")
            txtDoc(0).Enabled = (strCbo <> "Datas")

    End Select
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "cboDoc_Click()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub
Private Sub cboDoc_KeyPress(Index As Integer, KeyAscii As Integer)
    If KeyAscii = 13 Then Sendkeys "{TAB}"
End Sub


Private Sub cboVenda_Click(Index As Integer)
    Select Case cboVenda(1).Text
        Case "Conf. Encomenda"
            fraVenda(0).Enabled = False
            fraVenda(1).Enabled = False
            Frame2.Enabled = False
            txtVenda(13).Text = "0"
            txtVenda(12).Text = "0"
            txtVenda(7).Text = "0"
            '        Case "Factura Simplificada"
            '            Informacao.Show vbModal
        Case Else
            fraVenda(0).Enabled = True
            fraVenda(1).Enabled = True
            Frame2.Enabled = True
    End Select
End Sub

    If KeyAscii = 13 Then Sendkeys "{TAB}"
End Sub

Private Sub chkDoc_Click(Index As Integer)
    If Index = 1 Then
        If cboDoc(2).ListIndex = 1 Then
            txtDoc(1).Visible = (chkDoc(1).value = 1)
            txtDoc(1).Left = 15 + txtDoc(0).Left + txtDoc(0).Width
            txtDoc(1).MaxLength = txtDoc(0).MaxLength
            txtDoc(1).Width = txtDoc(0).Width
            txtDoc(1).Text = ""
        End If
    End If
End Sub

Private Sub chkDoc_KeyPress(Index As Integer, KeyAscii As Integer)
    If KeyAscii = 13 Then Sendkeys "{TAB}"
End Sub

Private Sub cmdApuroGeral_Click(Index As Integer)
    Dim strSQL As String, strFind As String
    Dim strCampo As String
    Dim bValorZero As Byte, bValorUm As Byte
    Dim bIndex As Byte
    Dim bActive As Boolean
    Dim iErro As Integer
    On Error GoTo erro
    Select Case Index
        Case 0    'periodo
            Dim x As New IBCalendar

            vPeriodo = x.Show(Date, True)

            If Not IsNull(vPeriodo) Then
                lblApuroGeral(1).Caption = vPeriodo(0) & " ate " & vPeriodo(1)
            Else
                lblApuroGeral(1).Caption = ""
            End If

        Case 1    'ok
            ' cmdApuroGeral(1).Tag = 1 controla se este foi escolhido.

            bValorZero = chkApuroGeral(0).value
            bValorUm = chkApuroGeral(1).value
            bIndex = cboApuroGeral(0).ListIndex + 1

            cmdApuroGeral(1).Tag = 1
            If bValorUm = 1 Then
                strCampo = " Where cabapTipoApuro = " & bIndex
            Else
                strFind = " cabapTipoApuro = " & bIndex
            End If

            If bValorZero = 1 Then
                strCampo = IIf(strCampo <> "", strCampo & " and ", " Where ") & "cabapDataInicio >= #" & Format(vPeriodo(0), "mm-dd-yyyy") & "# and cabapDataInicio <= #" & Format(vPeriodo(1), "mm-dd-yyyy") & "#"
            Else
                If strFind = "" Then
                    If lblApuroGeral(1).Caption <> "" Then
                        strFind = "cabapDataInicio = #" & Format(vPeriodo(0), "mm-dd-yyyy") & "#"
                    End If
                Else
                    If lblApuroGeral(1).Caption <> "" Then
                        strFind = strFind & " AND cabapDataInicio = #" & Format(vPeriodo(0), "mm-dd-yyyy") & "#"
                    End If
                End If

            End If

            If strCampo <> "" Then
                strSQL = "select * from qyCabApuros " & strCampo

                oUtils.CreateDataRecordset dbOptiware98, strSQL, datApuroGeral, dbOpenDynaset
                With tabApuros
                    .Tab = TABPosApurosApuro
                    .TabState = IIf(bActive Or NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_APUROS_APURO"), TAB_STATE_ENABLED, TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT)
                    .Tab = TABPosApurosMovimentos
                    .TabState = IIf(bActive Or NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_APUROS_MOV"), TAB_STATE_ENABLED, TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT)
                End With
            Else
                With datApuroGeral.Recordset
                    .FindFirst strFind
                End With
            End If
            bActive = (datApuroGeral.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)
            ActivaPesquisaPos Apuros, bActive
        Case 2    'Sair
            Unload Me

        Case 3    'Inserir
            If bArquivo() Then Exit Sub
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_APUROS_GERAL_NOVO") Then Exit Sub
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_APUROS_APURO") Then Exit Sub
            With tabApuros
                .Tag = 1    ' Novo Apuro
                .Tab = TABPosApurosMovimentos
                .TabState = TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT
                .Tab = TABPosApurosApuro
                .ActiveTab = TABPosApurosApuro
                .TabState = TAB_STATE_ENABLED
                .TabSetChildEnabled picApurosCx(0), True
                .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(1), False
                .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(0), False
                .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(7), False
            End With
            cmdApurosCx(8).Visible = False
            Set xaApurosCx = Nothing
            xaApurosCx.ReDim 0, 0, 0, 8
            tdgApurosCx.Array = xaApurosCx
            tdgApurosCx.ReBind
            lblApurosCX(2).Caption = ""
            cboApurosCX(0).ListIndex = 0

            Dim rs As Recordset

            oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, "qyCaixas", rs, dbOpenSnapshot
            With cboApurosCX(1)
                .Clear
                .AddItem "Global"
                Do While Not rs.EOF
                    .AddItem rs!cxNome
                    rs.MoveNext
                Loop
                rs.Close
                Set rs = Nothing
                .ListIndex = 0
            End With

        Case 4    'Imprimir
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_APUROS_GERAL_IMPRIMIR") Then Exit Sub
            ImpApurosResumo

        Case 5    ' Limpar
            oUtils.CreateDataRecordset dbOptiware98, "qyCabApuros", datApuroGeral, dbOpenSnapshot
            bActive = (datApuroGeral.Recordset.RecordCount > 0)
            With tabApuros
                .Tab = TABPosApurosApuro
                .TabState = IIf(bActive Or NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_APUROS_APURO"), TAB_STATE_ENABLED, TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT)
                .Tab = TABPosApurosMovimentos
                .TabState = IIf(bActive Or NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_APUROS_MOV"), TAB_STATE_ENABLED, TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT)
            End With
            lblApuroGeral(1).Caption = ""
            chkApuroGeral(0).value = 0
            chkApuroGeral(1).value = 0
            cboApuroGeral(0).ListIndex = 0
            cmdApuroGeral(1).Tag = 0
            ActivaPesquisaPos Apuros, bActive

    End Select
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "cmdApuroGeral_Click()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:      On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub cmdApuroMov_Click(Index As Integer)
    Select Case Index
        Case 0
            Unload Me
        Case 1
            ImpApuroMov
    End Select
End Sub

Private Sub cmdApurosCx_Click(Index As Integer)
    Dim sNameFile As String, sTime As String, sOriginal As String
    Dim bApurosMov As Boolean
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sPath As String

    On Error GoTo erro
    Select Case Index
        Case 0    ' Imprimir
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_APUROS_APURO_IMPRIMIR") Then Exit Sub
            ImpApuroCx

        Case 1    'Exportar
            If bArquivo() Then Exit Sub
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_APUROS_APURO_EXPORTAR") Then Exit Sub
            sPath = App.Path
            If (Right$(sPath, 1) <> "\") Then
                sPath = sPath & "\"
            End If
            sTime = Time
            sNameFile = sPath & Day(Date) & Month(Date) & Year(Date) & Format(Time, "hhmmss")
            sOriginal = sPath & sNameFile
            With cdgvendas
                .DialogTitle = "Ficheiro de Apuros"
                .Flags = cdlOFNHideReadOnly + cdlOFNLongNames
                .Filter = "Ficheiro de Texto (*.txt)|*.txt|"
                .FileName = sNameFile
                .ShowSave
                If (.FileName <> "") Then sNameFile = .FileName
                If sOriginal = .FileName Then Exit Sub
            End With
            Screen.MousePointer = vbHourglass
            ExportarFileText sNameFile
            Screen.MousePointer = vbDefault

        Case 2    'construir apuro
            If bArquivo() Then Exit Sub
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_APUROS_APURO_CONSTRUIRAPURO") Then Exit Sub
            If bSemaforo(bOpen) Then
                GravaApuroDeCaixa bApurosMov
                bSemaforo bClose
            End If
            tabApuros.TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(2), False

            With tabApuros
                .FireTabActivateEvent = False
                .TabSetChildEnabled picApuroGeral, True
                .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApuroGeral(4), True
                .Tab = TABPosApurosMovimentos
                .TabState = IIf(Not NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_APUROS_MOV") And bApurosMov, TAB_STATE_ENABLED, TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT)
                .FireTabActivateEvent = True
            End With

        Case 3    'Sair
            Unload Me

        Case 4    'Ok da pesquisa
            If aEuro(C_DataSistemaEuro) <> "" Then
                If CDate(vPeriodo(0)) < CDate(aEuro(C_DataSistemaEuro)) And CDate(vPeriodo(1)) >= CDate(aEuro(C_DataSistemaEuro)) Then
                    MsgBox "Não é possivel calcular o apuro de caixa, neste periodo." & vbCrLf & "Terá que escolher um periodo inferior a " & aEuro(C_DataSistemaEuro), vbInformation
                    With tabApuros
                        .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(2), False
                        .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(1), False
                        .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(0), False
                        .TabSetChildEnabled picApurosCx(0), True
                    End With
                    Exit Sub
                End If
            End If
            If tabApuros.Tag = 1 Then
                CalculoApurosCaixa
            End If

        Case 5    'Perido
            Dim x As New IBCalendar
            vPeriodo = x.Show(Date, True)
            If Not IsNull(vPeriodo) Then
                lblApurosCX(2).Caption = vPeriodo(0) & " ate " & vPeriodo(1)
            Else
                lblApurosCX(2).Caption = ""
            End If

        Case 6    ' limpar
            lblApurosCX(2).Caption = ""
            cmdApurosCx(4).Enabled = False
            cmdApurosCx(5).Enabled = True
            With cboApurosCX(0)
                .ListIndex = 0: .Enabled = True
            End With
            With cboApurosCX(1)
                .ListIndex = 0: .Enabled = True
            End With
            With tabApuros
                .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(2), False
                .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(1), False
                .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(0), False
                .TabSetChildEnabled picApurosCx(0), True
            End With
            Set xaApurosCx = Nothing
            xaApurosCx.ReDim 0, 0, 0, 8
            tdgApurosCx.Array = xaApurosCx
            tdgApurosCx.ReBind

        Case 7    ' Inserir
            If bArquivo() Then Exit Sub
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_APUROS_GERAL_NOVO") Then Exit Sub
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_APUROS_APURO") Then Exit Sub
            With tabApuros
                .Tag = 1    ' Novo Apuro
                .Tab = TABPosApurosMovimentos
                .TabState = TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT
                .Tab = TABPosApurosApuro
                .ActiveTab = TABPosApurosApuro
                .TabState = TAB_STATE_ENABLED
                .TabSetChildEnabled picApurosCx(0), True
                .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(1), False
                .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(0), False
                .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(7), False

            End With
            cmdApurosCx(8).Visible = False
            Set xaApurosCx = Nothing
            xaApurosCx.ReDim 0, 0, 0, 8
            tdgApurosCx.Array = xaApurosCx
            tdgApurosCx.ReBind
            lblApurosCX(2).Caption = ""
            cboApurosCX(0).ListIndex = 0

            Dim rs As Recordset

            oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, "qyCaixas", rs, dbOpenSnapshot
            With cboApurosCX(1)
                .Clear
                .AddItem "Global"
                Do While Not rs.EOF
                    .AddItem rs!cxNome
                    rs.MoveNext
                Loop
                rs.Close
                Set rs = Nothing
                .ListIndex = 0
            End With

        Case 8    ' Recalculo
            If bSemaforo(bOpen) Then
                If MsgBox("Confirma o (re)calculo do apuro?", vbInformation + vbYesNo + vbDefaultButton2) = vbYes Then
                    CalculoApurosCaixa True
                    GravaApuroDeCaixa True, True
                End If
                bSemaforo bClose
            End If
    End Select

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "cmdApurosCx_Click()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:      On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
    Screen.MousePointer = vbDefault
End Sub

Private Sub cmdCaixa_Click(Index As Integer)
    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sQy As String, sFind As String
    Dim xExclusivo As Byte, byteIndex As Byte

    Dim fActivo As Boolean

    Dim rsArmazens As Recordset
    Dim vLastExport As Variant

    Select Case Index
        Case 0    ' OK
            CarregaListaCaixas

        Case 1    ' Abertura
            If bArquivo() Then Exit Sub
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_CX_RESUMO_ABERTURA") Then Exit Sub

            Set rsArmazens = dbo.OpenRecordset("Armazens", dbOpenTable)
            With rsArmazens
                Do While Not .EOF
                    If IsDate(!armEFim) Then
                        If IsDate(vLastExport) Then
                            If (!armEFim > CDate(vLastExport)) Then
                                vLastExport = !armEFim
                            End If
                        Else
                            vLastExport = !armEFim
                        End If
                    End If
                    .MoveNext
                Loop
            End With
            Set rsArmazens = Nothing

            If IsDate(vLastExport) Then
                vLastExport = CDate(Format(vLastExport, "dd-mm-yyyy hh:nn:ss"))
                If (DateDiff("s", vLastExport, Now) <= 0) Then
                    MsgBox "Não é possível reabrir uma caixa com a data anterior à da última consolidação!", vbInformation, msgInformation
                    Exit Sub
                End If
            End If
            
            If OptiwareEx.AbreCaixa Then
                cmdCaixa(1).Enabled = False
                
                tabPos.Tab = 0
                tabPos.TabState = IIf(NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_ATEND"), TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT, TAB_STATE_ENABLED)
                tabPos.Tab = 1
                tabPos.TabState = IIf(NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_VALORESPAG"), TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT, TAB_STATE_ENABLED)
                tabPos.Tab = 2
                tabPos.TabState = IIf(NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_DOC"), TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT, TAB_STATE_ENABLED)
                tabCaixa.TabSetChildEnabled cmdCaixa(1), False
                tabCaixa.TabSetChildEnabled cmdCaixa(2), True

                fValidaAcessos = True
                
                With datCaixa.Recordset
                    RsRequery datCaixa.Recordset
                    If Not .EOF Then
                        .MoveLast
                    End If
                End With
            End If

        Case 2    ' Imprimir
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_CX_RESUMO_IMPRIMIR") Then Exit Sub
            ImpCaixaResumo

        Case 3    ' Abrir Gaveta
            If bArquivo() Then Exit Sub
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_CX_RESUMO_GAVETA") Then Exit Sub
            AbrirGavetaPOS mscPOS, True

        Case 4    ' sair
            Unload Me

        Case 5    'Escolha de periodo
            Dim x As New IBCalendar
            vPeriodo = x.Show(Date, True)
            If Not IsNull(vPeriodo) Then
                lblCaixa(2).Caption = vPeriodo(0) & " ate " & vPeriodo(1)
            Else
                lblCaixa(2).Caption = ""
            End If

        Case 6    ' Limpar
            InicializaListaCaixas
            
    End Select

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "cmdCaixa_Click()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub cmdCxDiaria_Click(Index As Integer)
    Dim Dummy As Integer
    Dim iErro As Integer

    On Error GoTo erro
    Select Case Index
        Case 0    'Imprimir

            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_CX_CXDIA_IMPRIMIR") Then Exit Sub
            ImpCaixaDia

        Case 1    'Fita de Caixa
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_CX_CXDIA_FITACX") Then Exit Sub
            Call tabCaixa_TabActivate(0)
            ImprimirFitaCaixa datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlCxID, datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlcxCaixaid
            'ImprimirFitaCaixa
        Case 2    'Reabertura
            If bArquivo() Then Exit Sub
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_CX_CXDIA_REABERTURA") Then Exit Sub
            If bSemaforo(bOpen) Then
                Dummy = MsgBox("Confirma a reabertura da caixa?", vbInformation + vbYesNo + vbDefaultButton2)
                If Dummy = vbYes Then
                    ReaberturaCaixa
                End If
                bSemaforo bClose
            End If

        Case 3    'Fechar Caixa
            If bArquivo() Then Exit Sub
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_CX_CXDIA_FECHOCX") Then Exit Sub
            If bSemaforo(bOpen) Then
                FechoCaixa
                bSemaforo bClose
            End If

        Case 4    'Sair
            Unload Me

        Case 5    ' Obs.
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_CX_CXDIA_OBS") Then Exit Sub
            With frmPosCxObs
                .CarregaOBS = "" & datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlcxObsFecho
                .lIdCaixa = datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlCxID
                .TextLocked = Not IsNull(datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlcxDataFecho)
                .Show vbModal
            End With
        Case 6
            If NaoTemAcesso(True, "VD_ACTIVIDADE_COMERCIAL") Then Exit Sub
            ImprimirActividadeComercial datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlcxDataAbertura, datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlCxID, datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlcxCaixaid
    End Select
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "cmdCxDiaria_Click()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub ImprimirActividadeComercial(dDate As Date, lIdCtrlCaixa As Long, lIdCaixa As Long)

    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sTableFormat As String, sTableHeader As String
    Dim vspImpressao As vsPrinter
    Dim sNomeListagem As String

    Dim sImpressao As String
    Dim sSQLCondicao
    Dim sTipopag As String

    Dim rsDetalheVendas As Recordset
    Dim rsMovimentosCaixa As Recordset
    Dim rsDetalheDocumentos As Recordset
    Dim rsResumoFechoCaixa As Recordset
    Dim rsClientesNovos As Recordset
    Dim rsOptometriasNovas As Recordset
    Dim rsContactologiasNovas As Recordset
    Dim rsVendasDia As Recordset

    Dim lTotqtVendas As Double
    Dim lTotvalorVendas As Double
    Dim lTotValorIvaVendas As Double
    Dim lTotDescontosVendas As Double
    Dim lTotCompVendas As Double
    Dim lTotPMVendas As Double
    Dim lTotvalorMcx As Double
    Dim lTotDCValor As Double
    Dim lTotDCDesconto As Double
    Dim lTotDCComp As Double
    Dim lTotDCIVA As Double
    Dim lTotResumo As Double
    Dim lTotResumoInt As Double

    Set rsDetalheVendas = dbo.OpenRecordset("SELECT * FROM qyaDetalheVendasFamilia WHERE expr2 = #" & Format(dDate, "MM-DD-YYYY") & "# and CaixaID = " & lIdCaixa, dbOpenSnapshot)
    
    Set rsDetalheDocumentos = dbo.OpenRecordset("SELECT * FROM qyaDetalheDocumentos WHERE data = " & "#" & Format(dDate, "MM-DD-YYYY") & "#" & " and CaixaID = " & lIdCaixa, dbOpenSnapshot)
    Set rsResumoFechoCaixa = dbo.OpenRecordset("SELECT * FROM qyaFechoCaixa WHERE expr21 = " & lIdCtrlCaixa & " and CaixaID = " & lIdCaixa, dbOpenSnapshot)
    Set rsClientesNovos = dbo.OpenRecordset("SELECT * FROM qyaClientesNovos WHERE expr1 = " & "#" & Format(dDate, "MM-DD-YYYY") & "#", dbOpenSnapshot)
    Set rsOptometriasNovas = dbo.OpenRecordset("SELECT * FROM qyaOptometriasnovas WHERE oficDataFicha = " & "#" & Format(dDate, "MM-DD-YYYY") & "#", dbOpenSnapshot)
    Set rsContactologiasNovas = dbo.OpenRecordset("SELECT * FROM qyaContactologiasNovas WHERE cficDataFicha = " & "#" & Format(dDate, "MM-DD-YYYY") & "#", dbOpenSnapshot)
    Set rsVendasDia = dbo.OpenRecordset("SELECT * FROM ControleCaixa WHERE ctrlcxDataAbertura = " & "#" & Format(dDate, "MM-DD-YYYY") & "#" & " and ctrlcxCaixaId = " & lIdCaixa, dbOpenSnapshot)

    On Error GoTo erro

    With frmPrintPreview
        .impressora = ImpressoraListagens
    End With
    Set vspImpressao = frmPrintPreview.vspPreview

    sNomeListagem = "Relatório de Actividade Comercial"

    With vspImpressao
        .PageBorder = pbBottom
        .FontName = "Arial"
        .FontSize = 8
        .FontBold = False
        .FontItalic = False
        .Footer = "||Página %d"
        .MarginTop = 600
        .MarginBottom = 650
        .MarginLeft = 1000
        .MarginRight = 600
        .TextAlign = taLeftBaseline
        .TextAngle = 0
        .CurrentX = 300
        .Preview = True
    End With

    With vspImpressao
        .Orientation = orPortrait
        .StartDoc
        
        ImpressaoDoCabecalho vspImpressao, ImpressoraListagens
        
        vspImpressao.FontSize = 14
        vspImpressao.FontBold = True
        vspImpressao.CurrentX = 6000
        vspImpressao.CurrentY = 600
        vspImpressao.Paragraph = sNomeListagem
        vspImpressao.CurrentX = 9500
        vspImpressao.CurrentY = 900
        vspImpressao.FontSize = 10
        vspImpressao.Paragraph = Trim(dDate)
        vspImpressao.Paragraph = " "
        vspImpressao.FontBold = False
        vspImpressao.CurrentX = 1000
        vspImpressao.CurrentY = 2800
        vspImpressao.FontSize = 12
        vspImpressao.FontBold = True
        vspImpressao.Paragraph = "Detalhe das Vendas"
        vspImpressao.FontBold = False
        vspImpressao.FontSize = 8
        sTableFormat = "<+2400|>+900|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200"
        sTableHeader = "Familia|Total Qt.|Total Valor|Total IVA|Total Desc.|Total Comp.|Preço Médio"
        vspImpressao.AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        lTotqtVendas = 0
        lTotvalorVendas = 0
        lTotValorIvaVendas = 0
        lTotDescontosVendas = 0
        lTotCompVendas = 0
        lTotPMVendas = 0

        With rsDetalheVendas
            If Not .EOF Then
                Do While Not .EOF
                    sImpressao = !expr1 & "|" & Round(!totalquantidade) & "|" & Format(!totalvalor, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(!TotalIVA, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(!TotalDescontos, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(!TotalComparticipacao, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(!precomedio, "##,##0.00€")
                    vspImpressao.AddTable sTableFormat, vbNullString, sImpressao
                    lTotqtVendas = lTotqtVendas + !totalquantidade
                    lTotvalorVendas = lTotvalorVendas + !totalvalor
                    lTotValorIvaVendas = lTotValorIvaVendas + !TotalIVA
                    lTotDescontosVendas = lTotDescontosVendas + !TotalDescontos
                    lTotCompVendas = lTotCompVendas + !TotalComparticipacao
                    lTotPMVendas = lTotPMVendas + !precomedio
                    .MoveNext
                Loop
                sImpressao = "Total Global|" & Round(lTotqtVendas) & "|" & Format(lTotvalorVendas, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(lTotValorIvaVendas, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(lTotDescontosVendas, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(lTotCompVendas, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(lTotPMVendas, "##,##0.00€")
                vspImpressao.AddTable sTableFormat, vbNullString, sImpressao
            End If
        End With
        
        '
        ' Detalhe de Movimentos de Caixa
        '
        vspImpressao.Paragraph = " "
        vspImpressao.FontSize = 12
        vspImpressao.FontBold = True
        vspImpressao.Paragraph = "Detalhe de Movimentos de Caixa"
        vspImpressao.FontBold = False
        vspImpressao.FontSize = 8
        sTableFormat = "<+1500|<+3000|>+1300|>+1300|^+900|>+2200"
        sTableHeader = "Operador|Descrição|Obra/Doc|Valor|T. Mov.|Forma Pag."
        vspImpressao.AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        lTotvalorMcx = 0

        Set rsMovimentosCaixa = dbo.OpenRecordset( _
            "SELECT * FROM qyaMovCaixa WHERE Data = " & SqlDate(dDate) & " and CaixaID = " & lIdCaixa, _
            dbOpenSnapshot)
            
        With rsMovimentosCaixa
            If Not .EOF Then
                Do While Not .EOF
                    Select Case !TipoPag
                        Case 1
                            sTipopag = "Numerário"
                        Case 2
                            sTipopag = "Cheque"
                        Case 3
                            sTipopag = "Multibanco"
                        Case 4
                            sTipopag = "Cartao de Crédito"
                        Case 5
                            sTipopag = "Nota de Crédito"
                        Case 6
                            sTipopag = "Multiplo Pagamento"
                        Case 7
                            sTipopag = "Transferência"
                        Case Else
                            sTipopag = " "
                    End Select
                    
                    sImpressao = !Creator & "|" & !descricao & "|" & !NumDoc & "|" & Format(!valor, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & !tipo & "|" & sTipopag
                    vspImpressao.AddTable sTableFormat, vbNullString, sImpressao
                    
                    If !tipo = "C" Then
                        lTotvalorMcx = lTotvalorMcx + !valor
                    ElseIf !tipo = "D" Then
                        lTotvalorMcx = lTotvalorMcx - !valor
                    End If
                    
                    .MoveNext
                Loop
                sImpressao = "|" & "Total de Movimentos|" & "|" & Format(lTotvalorMcx, "##,##0.00€") & "|"
                vspImpressao.AddTable sTableFormat, vbNullString, sImpressao
            End If
        End With

        vspImpressao.NewPage
        vspImpressao.FontBold = True
        vspImpressao.FontSize = 12
        vspImpressao.Paragraph = "Estatistica de Clientes/Consultas "
        vspImpressao.FontSize = 8
        vspImpressao.Paragraph = " "
        With rsClientesNovos
            If Not .EOF Then
                vspImpressao.Paragraph = "Nº Clientes Novos: " & !numclientes
            Else
                vspImpressao.Paragraph = "Nº Clientes Novos: " & "0"
            End If
        End With

        With rsOptometriasNovas
            If Not .EOF Then
                vspImpressao.Paragraph = "Nº Optometrias Novas: " & !numoptometrias
            Else
                vspImpressao.Paragraph = "Nº Optometrias Novas: " & "0"
            End If
        End With

        With rsContactologiasNovas
            If Not .EOF Then
                vspImpressao.Paragraph = "Nº Contactologias Novas: " & !numcontactologias
            Else
                vspImpressao.Paragraph = "Nº Contactologias Novas: " & "0"
            End If
        End With
        vspImpressao.FontBold = False

        vspImpressao.Paragraph = " "
        vspImpressao.FontSize = 12
        vspImpressao.FontBold = True
        vspImpressao.Paragraph = "Detalhe de Documentos"
        vspImpressao.FontBold = False
        vspImpressao.FontSize = 8

        sTableFormat = "<+1800|^+1100|>+900|<+1200|>+900|>+900|>+900|>+900|<+900"
        sTableHeader = "Tipo de Documento|Data|Numero|Entidade|Valor|Desconto|Comp.|IVA|Estado"
        vspImpressao.AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        lTotDCValor = 0
        lTotDCDesconto = 0
        lTotDCComp = 0
        lTotDCIVA = 0

        With rsDetalheDocumentos

            If Not .EOF Then
                Do While Not .EOF
                    sImpressao = !tipoDoc & "|" & !Data & "|" & !Numero & "|" & !Entidade & "|" & Format(!Total, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(!Desconto, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(!Compart, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(!ValorIVA, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & !Estado
                    vspImpressao.AddTable sTableFormat, vbNullString, sImpressao
                    lTotDCValor = lTotDCValor + !Total
                    lTotDCDesconto = lTotDCDesconto + !Desconto
                    lTotDCComp = lTotDCComp + !Compart
                    lTotDCIVA = lTotDCIVA + !ValorIVA
                    .MoveNext
                Loop
                sImpressao = "Totais|" & "|" & "|" & "|" & Format(lTotDCValor, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(lTotDCDesconto, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(lTotDCComp, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(lTotDCIVA, "##,##0.00€") & "|"
                vspImpressao.AddTable sTableFormat, vbNullString, sImpressao
            End If
        End With

        vspImpressao.Paragraph = " "
        vspImpressao.FontSize = 12
        vspImpressao.FontBold = True
        vspImpressao.Paragraph = "Resumo do Fecho de Caixa"
        vspImpressao.FontBold = False
        vspImpressao.FontSize = 8
        sTableFormat = "<+2100|>+1200|>+1200|>+1200"
        sTableHeader = "Tipos de Pagamento|Valores de Caixa|Valores Inseridos|Diferença"
        vspImpressao.AddTable sTableFormat, sTableHeader, vbNullString, &HE0E0E0

        lTotResumo = 0
        lTotResumoInt = 0

        With rsResumoFechoCaixa
            If Not .EOF Then
                sImpressao = "Numerário" & "|" & Format(!expr2, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(!expr7, "##,##0.00€") & "|" & Format(!expr7 - !expr2, "##,##0.00€")
                vspImpressao.AddTable sTableFormat, vbNullString, sImpressao
