Private Sub tabApuros_TabPageShown(ActiveTab As Integer, ActivePage As Integer)
    Dim bx As Boolean
    Dim dDate1 As Date
    Dim dDate2 As Date
    Dim iErro As Integer

    On Error GoTo erro

    Select Case ActiveTab
        Case 0    'Apuros Geral
            With datApuroGeral
                If oUtils.Convert2Long(.Tag) = 1 Then
                    .Recordset.Requery
                    bx = .Recordset.RecordCount <> 0
                    With tabApuros
                        .FireTabActivateEvent = False
                        .TabSetChildEnabled picApuroGeral, bx
                        .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApuroGeral(4), bx
                        .Tab = 1
                        .TabState = IIf(bx And Not NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_APUROS_APURO"), TAB_STATE_ENABLED, TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT)
                        .Tab = 2
                        .TabState = IIf(bx And Not NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_APUROS_MOV"), TAB_STATE_ENABLED, TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT)
                        .FireTabActivateEvent = True
                    End With
                End If
            End With
            tabApuros.Tag = 0
            cboApuroGeral(0).ListIndex = IIf(cboApuroGeral(0).ListIndex = -1, 0, cboApuroGeral(0).ListIndex)

        Case 1    'Apuros de caixa
            If oUtils.Convert2Integer(tabApuros.Tag) <> 0 Then    'Consulta de um apuro
                fraApuros.Caption = "Pesquisar"
            Else
                cmdApurosCx(8).Visible = True
                ConsultaApurosCX
                fraApuros.Caption = "Dados no Apuro"
                cmdApurosCx(4).Enabled = False
                With tabApuros
                    .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(2), False
                    .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(1), True
                    .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(0), True
                    .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApurosCx(7), True
                    .TabSetChildEnabled picApurosCx(0), False
                End With
                With datApuroGeral.Recordset
                    'cboApurosCX(0).Text = !xTipo
                    cboApurosCX(1).AddItem !xCaixa
                    cboApurosCX(1).ListIndex = 0
                    lblApurosCX(2).Caption = Format(!cabapDataInicio, "dd-mm-yyyy") & " ate " & Format(!cabapdatafim, "dd-mm-yyyy")
                End With

            End If

        Case 2    'Movimentos
            If tabApuros.Tag = 0 Then
                With datApuroGeral.Recordset
                    dDate1 = !cabapDataInicio
                    dDate2 = !cabapdatafim
                End With
            Else
                dDate1 = vPeriodo(0)
                dDate2 = vPeriodo(1)
            End If

            CalculoMovimentosCx dDate1, dDate2

    End Select
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "tabApuros_TabPageShown()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub tabCaixa_TabActivate(TabToActivate As Integer)

    Dim lidControleCaixa As Long, lIdCaixa As Long
    Dim dData As Date
    Dim sSQL As String
    Dim Mybook As Variant
    Dim rs As Recordset
    Dim fActiva As Boolean, fCaixa As Boolean
    Dim iErro As Integer

    On Error GoTo erro

    lidControleCaixa = oUtils.Convert2Long(tabCaixa.Tag)

    Select Case TabToActivate
        Case TABPosCaixaResumo    ' Resumo de caixa
            If oUtils.Convert2Long(datCaixa.Tag) = 1 Then
                With datCaixa.Recordset
                    RsRequery datCaixa.Recordset
                    .FindFirst "ctrlcxId = " & lidControleCaixa
                End With
            End If
            cboCaixa(0).ListIndex = IIf(cboCaixa(0).ListIndex = -1, 0, cboCaixa(0).ListIndex)
            ActivaBotoesPos ResumeCaixa, (datCaixa.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)

        Case TABPosCaixaDia    'Caixa do Dia
            With datCaixa.Recordset
                If .RecordCount <> 0 Then Carrega_CaixadoDia
                ValidaValoresIntroduzir
                ActivaBotoesPos CaixaDoDia, (.RecordCount <> 0)
            End With

            If aUser(20) Then fraCaixaDiaria(0).Visible = False

        Case TABPosCaixaVendas    'Vendas



            fActiva = (datCaixa.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)
            If oUtils.Convert2Long(datCaixaVenda.Tag) = 0 Then
                If fActiva Then
                    dData = datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlcxDataAbertura
                    lIdCaixa = datCaixa.Recordset!ctrlcxCaixaid
                    oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, "Select sum(cabvenTotal) - sum(cabvenTotDescontos) - sum(cabvenTotComp) as xTotal from qyVendasCaixa where CabVenEstado=0 and CabVenIdCaixa=" & lIdCaixa & " and cabvenData = #" & Format(dData, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "#", rs, dbOpenSnapshot
                    With rs
                        If .RecordCount >= 1 Then
                            lblTxtVendas.Caption = Format(!xTotal, "Standard")
                        End If
                    End With
                    Set rs = Nothing

                    'Modificado para correcção do erro nº 0083
                    'oUtils.CreateDataRecordset dbOptiware98, "select * from qyVendasCaixa where CabVenIdCaixa=" & lIdCaixa & " and cabvenData = #" & Format(dData, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "#", datCaixaVenda, dbOpenSnapshot

                    sSQL = "SELECT * FROM qyVendasCaixa WHERE cabvenIDCaixa = " & lIdCaixa & " AND " & _
                           "cabvenData = #" & Format$(dData, "mm-dd-yyyy") & "# AND " & _
                           "cabvenEstado = 0 ORDER BY CabVenNumVenda"
                    oUtils.CreateDataRecordset dbOptiware98, sSQL, datCaixaVenda, dbOpenSnapshot
                    datCaixaVenda.Tag = 1
                    fActiva = (datCaixaVenda.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)
                End If
            Else
                datCaixaVenda.Recordset.Requery
                fActiva = (datCaixaVenda.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)
            End If
            ActivaBotoesPos IIf(tabVendas.ActiveTab = 0, VendasCaixa, VendasCaixaDetalhe), fActiva

            If aUser(20) Then
                tabVendas.FireTabActivateEvent = False
                tabVendas.Tab = 1
                tabVendas.TabState = 2
                tabVendas.FireTabActivateEvent = True
            End If

        Case TABPosCaixaMovimentos    'Movimentos
            fCaixa = (datCaixa.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)
            If oUtils.Convert2Long(datCaixaMov.Tag) = 0 Then
                If fCaixa Then
                    oUtils.CreateDataRecordset dbOptiware98, "select * From qyMovCaixaCx WHERE mcxControleCaixaId = " & lidControleCaixa, datCaixaMov, dbOpenDynaset
                    fActiva = (datCaixaMov.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)
                    datCaixaMov.Tag = 1
                End If
            Else
                datCaixaMov.Recordset.Requery
                fActiva = (datCaixaMov.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)
            End If


            Dim dSaldo As Double

            oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, "Select Sum(xCredito)- Sum(xDebito) as XSaldo from qyMovCaixaCxSaldo Where mcxControleCaixaId = " & lidControleCaixa, rs, dbOpenSnapshot
            If rs.RecordCount >= 0 Then
                dSaldo = oUtils.Convert2Double(rs!xSaldo)
                lblCxMov(0).Caption = Format$(dSaldo, "Standard")
            End If
            Set rs = Nothing
            ActivaBotoesPos MovimentosCaixa, fActiva, fCaixa

        Case TABPosCaixaVales    'Vales
            fCaixa = (datCaixa.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)

            If oUtils.Convert2Long(datCaixaVales.Tag) = 0 Then

                '*************************************************
                'Changed By: Paulo Mourão
                'Date:       21-10-1999 17:16:19
                'Linha modificada pelo erro nº 0085
                'oUtils.CreateDataRecordset dbOptiware98, "select * from qyVales Where valControleCaixaId =" & lidControleCaixa, datCaixaVales, dbOpenDynaset
                '*************************************************
                oUtils.CreateDataRecordset dbOptiware98, "select * from qyVales;", datCaixaVales, dbOpenDynaset
                datCaixaVales.Tag = 1
                fActiva = (datCaixaVales.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)
            Else
                datCaixaVales.Recordset.Requery
                fActiva = (datCaixaVales.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)
            End If

            ActivaBotoesPos ValesCaixa, fActiva, fCaixa

    End Select

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "tabCaixa_TabActivate()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub tabCaixa_TabPageShown(ActiveTab As Integer, ActivePage As Integer)

    Dim fVisible As Boolean
    Dim iCount As Integer

    If (ActiveTab = 0) Then
        fVisible = Not NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_CX_RESUMO_DETALHES_RESUMO")
        With tdgCaixa
            For iCount = 3 To 9
                .Columns(iCount).Visible = fVisible
            Next
        End With
    End If

End Sub


Private Sub tabPos_TabActivate(TabToActivate As Integer)
    Debug_EscreveLinha "frmPosMain.tabPos_TabActivate " & TabToActivate
    On Error GoTo erro

    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim lIdCaixa As Long
    Dim fActiva As Boolean
    Dim lLastNumber As Long
    Dim myRs As Recordset
    Dim fDummy As Boolean

    Select Case TabToActivate
        Case TABPosAtendimento    'Vendas

            'oUtils.CreateRecordset dbOptiware98, "Contadores", myRs, dbOpenTable
            lLastNumber = oUtils.Convert2Long(rsContadores!conNumeroVenda) + 1
            'myRs.Close
            'Set myRs = Nothing
            txtVenda(0).Text = lLastNumber

            Dim vDoc As Variant
            fDummy = oRegistry.GetRegValue(HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE, "Software\Optiware98", "DefaultDocFS", REG_SZ, vDoc)
            If fDummy = True Then
                cboVenda(1).ListIndex = 1
            End If

        Case TABPosCreditos    'Creditos
            CarregaCreditos

            

        Case TABPosDocumentos    'Documentos

            If oUtils.Convert2Long(datDoc.Tag) = 0 Then
                oUtils.CreateDataRecordset dbOptiware98, "SELECT * FROM qyCabDoc ORDER BY cabdocData DESC, xTipoDoc, NumDoc DESC", datDoc, dbOpenDynaset
                datDoc.Tag = 1
            Else
                If datDoc.Recordset.RecordCount > 0 Then
                    datDoc.Recordset.MoveLast
                    datDoc.Recordset.MoveFirst
                    datDoc.Recordset.Requery
                End If
            End If
            cboDoc(0).ListIndex = IIf(cboDoc(0).ListIndex = -1, 0, cboDoc(0).ListIndex)
            cboDoc(1).ListIndex = IIf(cboDoc(1).ListIndex = -1, 0, cboDoc(1).ListIndex)
            cboDoc(2).ListIndex = IIf(cboDoc(2).ListIndex = -1, 0, cboDoc(2).ListIndex)
            fActiva = (datDoc.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)
            ActivaBotoesPos Documentos, fActiva
            ActivaPesquisaPos Documentos, fActiva
            byDocumentos = Documentos
            
            
            
            OptiwareEx.RegistaOperacao "Vendas.Documentos.Listar"

        Case TABPosCaixa    'Caixa6
            If cboCaixa(0).ListIndex < 0 Then
                cboCaixa(0).ListIndex = 0
            End If
            
            If oUtils.Convert2Long(datCaixa.Tag) = 0 Then
                CarregaListaCaixas
            Else
                lIdCaixa = oUtils.Convert2Long(tabCaixa.Tag)
                With datCaixa.Recordset
                    RsRequery datCaixa.Recordset
                    .FindFirst "ctrlcxId = " & lIdCaixa
                End With
            End If
            
            With datCaixa.Recordset
                If .RecordCount <> 0 Then
                    Select Case tabCaixa.ActiveTab
                        Case TABPosCaixaVendas    'Vendas
                            datCaixaVenda.Recordset.Requery
                        Case TABPosCaixaMovimentos    'Movimentos
                            datCaixaMov.Recordset.Requery
                        Case TABPosCaixaVales    'vales
                            datCaixaVales.Recordset.Requery
                    End Select
                End If
            End With
            
            ActualizaVisibilidadeColunasCaixa

        Case TABPosApuros  'Apuros
            If oUtils.Convert2Long(datApuroGeral.Tag) = 0 Then
                oUtils.CreateDataRecordset dbOptiware98, "qyCabApuros", datApuroGeral, dbOpenSnapshot
                With datApuroGeral
                    .Tag = 1
                    fActiva = .Recordset.RecordCount <> 0
                End With
                With tabApuros
                    .FireTabActivateEvent = False
                    .TabSetChildEnabled picApuroGeral, fActiva
                    .TabSetChildEnabled cmdApuroGeral(4), fActiva
                    .Tab = TABPosApurosApuro
                    .TabState = IIf(fActiva And Not NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_APUROS_APURO"), TAB_STATE_ENABLED, TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT)
                    .Tab = TABPosApurosMovimentos
                    .TabState = IIf(fActiva And Not NaoTemAcesso(False, "VD_APUROS_MOV"), TAB_STATE_ENABLED, TAB_STATE_DISABLED_TEXT)
                    .FireTabActivateEvent = True
                End With
            Else
                datApuroGeral.Recordset.Requery
            End If
            fActiva = (datApuroGeral.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)
            ActivaBotoesPos Apuros, fActiva
            ActivaPesquisaPos Apuros, fActiva
            tabApuros.ActiveTab = TABPosApurosResumo

    End Select

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "tabPos_TabPageShown()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub tabVendas_TabActivate(TabToActivate As Integer)

    Dim iTag As Integer
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim fActiva As Boolean

    On Error GoTo erro

    Screen.MousePointer = vbHourglass

    Select Case TabToActivate
        Case 0  'Vendas do Dia

            With datCaixaVenda.Recordset
                RsRequery datCaixaVenda.Recordset
                fActiva = (.RecordCount <> 0)
            End With

            ActivaBotoesPos VendasCaixa, fActiva
            cmdVendas(0).Left = 0
            cmdVendas(2).Visible = True

        Case 1

            If CarregaCaixas_DetalheVendas(cboCxVendasGeral(1)) Then Exit Sub

            iTag = oUtils.Convert2Integer(datCxVendasGeral(0).Tag)

            If (iTag = 0) Then
                IniPesquisaCxVendasGeral
            Else
                datCxVendasGeral(0).Recordset.Requery
                fActiva = (datCxVendasGeral(0).Recordset.RecordCount <> 0)
            End If

            ActivaBotoesPos VendasCaixaDetalhe, fActiva
            ActivaPesquisaPos VendasCaixaDetalhe, fActiva

    End Select

    Screen.MousePointer = vbDefault

    Exit Sub

erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "tabVendas_TabActivate()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub tdgCreditos_FetchRowStyle(ByVal Split As Integer, bookmark As Variant, ByVal RowStyle As TrueDBGrid50.StyleDisp)
    Dim Data As Date, facturado As String, Situacao As Variant
    Data = CDate(tdgCreditos.Columns("Data").CellValue(bookmark))
    facturado = CStr(tdgCreditos.Columns("Doc").CellValue(bookmark))
        
    If DateDiff("d", Data, Date) > 31 And facturado <> "" Then  'And (Situacao = OFC_ENTREGUE Or Situacao = "")
        RowStyle.ForeColor = RGB(176, 0, 0) ' Vermelho
    ElseIf DateDiff("d", Data, Date) > 15 And facturado = "" Then  ' And (Situacao = OFC_PRONTA_ENTREGA Or Situacao = "")
        RowStyle.ForeColor = RGB(176, 144, 0) ' Amarelo
    End If
End Sub

Private Sub tdgCreditos_HeadClick(ByVal ColIndex As Integer)
    Dim iErro As Integer
    On Error GoTo erro

    iFlagCreditos = 0
    
    Dim Col As Column
    
    With tdgCreditos
        Select Case .Columns(ColIndex).Caption
            Case "Data", "Obra", "Venda", "Doc", "Cliente", "ReferenciaExterna"
                sOrderCreditos = .Columns(ColIndex).Caption
                            
                For Each Col In .Columns
                    Col.HeadFont.Bold = False
                Next Col
            
                .Columns(ColIndex).HeadFont.Bold = True
                CarregaCreditos
        End Select
    End With

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "tdgCreditos_HeadClick()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose

End Sub

Private Sub tdgCreditos_KeyPress(KeyAscii As Integer)
    If KeyAscii = vbKeySpace Then
        iFlagCreditos = 1
        tdgCreditos.PostMsg IdMsgUpdate
    Else
        KeyAscii = 0
    End If
End Sub

Private Sub tdgCreditos_MouseUp(Button As Integer, Shift As Integer, x As Single, Y As Single)
    Dim iLinhas As Long
    Dim iLinhasNew As Long
    Dim iErro As Integer
    On Error GoTo erro
    If datCreditos.Recordset.RecordCount <> 0 Then
        iFlagCreditos = 1
        With tdgCreditos
            iLinhas = .Row
            iLinhasNew = .RowContaining(Y)
            If .ColContaining(x) = 0 And iLinhas = iLinhasNew Then
                .PostMsg IdMsgUpdate
            End If
        End With
    End If
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "tdgCreditos_MouseUp()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

    Select Case MsgId
        Case IdMsgUpdate
            ValidaMarcacao
    End Select

End Sub

        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar

    End Select

Private Sub tdgCreditos_UnboundColumnFetch(bookmark As Variant, ByVal Col As Integer, value As Variant)
    Dim colInfo As Column
    Set colInfo = tdgCreditos.Columns(Col)
    
    Select Case colInfo.Caption
        Case "Doc"
            Select Case tdgCreditos.Columns("cdVenFacturada").CellValue(bookmark)
                Case 0
                    value = ""
                Case DOC_CLIENTE_FACTURA
                    value = "FT"
                Case DOC_CLIENTE_FACTURA_SIMPLIFICADA
                    value = "FS"
                Case DOC_CLIENTE_FACTURARECIBO
                    value = "FR"
                Case DOC_CLIENTE_VENDA_DINHEIRO
                    value = "VD"
                Case DOC_CLIENTE_NOTA_CREDITO
                    value = "NC"
                Case Else
                    value = "?"
            End Select
    End Select
End Sub

    If oUtils.Convert2Long(datCaixaVenda.Tag) <> 0 Then
        If datCaixaVenda.Recordset.RecordCount > 0 Then tdgCxVendas.Tag = datCaixaVenda.Recordset!cabvenid
    End If
End Sub

        RowStyle.value = "Anuladas"
    End If
End Sub

Private Sub tdgVenda_AfterDelete()

    Dim dDesconto As Double, dSomaValores As Double
    Dim dTotalValor As Double, dPreco As Double
    Dim iQt As Integer, iRow As Integer
    Dim iErro As Integer
    On Error GoTo erro
    tdgVenda.Update
    dTotalValor = 0
    With xaVendas
        For iRow = .LowerBound(1) To .UpperBound(1)
            iQt = .value(iRow, 2)
            dPreco = .value(iRow, 4)
            dTotalValor = iQt * dPreco + dTotalValor
            If tdgVenda.Columns(5).Caption = "Desc. %" Then
                dDesconto = dDesconto + oUtils.Convert2Double(.value(iRow, 5)) / 100 * iQt * dPreco
            Else
                dDesconto = dDesconto + oUtils.Convert2Double(.value(iRow, 5))
            End If
        Next iRow
    End With

    lblTotais(0).Caption = Format$(dTotalValor, "Standard")
    dTotalValor = dTotalValor - dDesconto
    lblTotais(1).Caption = Format$(dTotalValor, "Standard")
    lblTotais(2).Caption = Format$(dDesconto, "Standard")
    dSomaValores = edValores.Total
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "tdgVenda_AfterDelete()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub tdgVenda_BeforeColEdit(ByVal ColIndex As Integer, ByVal KeyAscii As Integer, Cancel As Integer)
    Dim iErro As Integer
    On Error GoTo erro
    Cancel = True
    If ActivaIntroducaoVendas(ColIndex, KeyAscii) Then Exit Sub
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "tdgVenda_BeforeColEdit()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Property Get DescontosEmPercentagem() As Boolean
    DescontosEmPercentagem = (tdgVenda.Columns(5).Caption = "Desc. %")
End Property

Private Property Let DescontosEmPercentagem(ByVal perc As Boolean)
    Dim lLinha As Long, lColuna As Long
    Dim dNovoDesconto As Double, dValor As Double
    
    ' Actualiza valores
    With tdgVenda
        lLinha = .Row
        lColuna = .Col
    End With
    
    Dim lContador As Long, linha As VendaLinha
    For lContador = 0 To xaVendas.UpperBound(1)
        Set linha = ObtemLinha(lContador)
        If perc Then
            xaVendas(lContador, 5) = Format$(linha.DescontoPercentagem, "Standard")
        Else
            xaVendas(lContador, 5) = Format$(linha.Desconto, "Standard")
        End If
    Next

    With tdgVenda
        .ReBind
        .Row = lLinha
        .Col = lColuna
    End With
    
    ' Actualiza cabeçalho
    With tdgVenda.Columns(5)
        If perc Then
            .Caption = "Desc. %"
        Else
            If C_MoedaSistemaEscudos Then
                .Caption = "Desc. $"
            Else
                .Caption = "Desc. €"
            End If
        End If
    End With
    
    ' Recalcula totais
    Cal_QtPreco
End Property

Private Sub tdgVenda_HeadClick(ByVal ColIndex As Integer)
    Select Case ColIndex
        Case 5
            DescontosEmPercentagem = Not DescontosEmPercentagem
    End Select
End Sub

Private Sub tdgVenda_KeyPress(KeyAscii As Integer)
    Dim iRow As Integer
    Dim lCurrentRow As Long
    Dim iUltimo As Integer
    If KeyAscii = 13 And tdgVenda.Col = 5 Then
        lCurrentRow = tdgVenda.Row
        tdgVenda.MoveLast
        iUltimo = tdgVenda.Row
        tdgVenda.Row = lCurrentRow
        If lCurrentRow < iUltimo + 1 Then
            tdgVenda.Row = iRow + 1
        End If
        tdgVenda.Col = 0
    End If
End Sub

Private Sub tdgVenda_PostEvent(ByVal MsgId As Integer)
    Select Case MsgId
        Case IdMsgUpdate
            tdgVenda.Update
    End Select
End Sub

Private Sub timObservacoes_Timer()

    Dim lColor As Long

    With timObservacoes
        Select Case .Tag
            Case "1"
                .Tag = "2"
                lColor = vbButtonFace
            Case "2"
                .Tag = "1"
                lColor = vbWhite
        End Select
    End With

    cmdCredito(2).BackColor = lColor

End Sub

Private Sub txtCxDiaria_GotFocus(Index As Integer)

    Dim lDummy As Boolean
    Dim sAux As String
    Dim iErro As Integer

    On Error GoTo erro

    oValidate.OnGotFocus txtCxDiaria(Index)
    If Index > 0 Then
        lDummy = oUtils.FormatNumber(txtCxDiaria(Index).Text, 2, 0, sDecSeparador, sMilSeparador, sAux)
        txtCxDiaria(Index).Text = sAux
    End If
    
    With txtCxDiaria(Index)
        .SelStart = 0
        .SelLength = Len(.Text)
    End With

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "txtCxDiaria_GotFocus()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub txtCxDiaria_KeyPress(Index As Integer, KeyAscii As Integer)
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim iPos As Integer

    On Error GoTo erro

    If KeyAscii = 13 Then Sendkeys "{TAB}"
    If Index > 0 Then
        With txtCxDiaria(Index)
            iPos = .SelStart
            oValidate.ValidNumber .Text, sDecSeparador, KeyAscii, iPos, 9, 2
            If .SelStart <> iPos Then
                .SelStart = iPos
            End If
        End With
    End If

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "txtCxDiaria_KeyPress()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub txtCxDiaria_LostFocus(Index As Integer)
    Dim lDummy As Boolean
    Dim xlbl As Double, xlblTotal As Double
    Dim xtxt As Double, xtxtTotal As Double
    Dim xObjTxt As TextBox
    Dim sAux As String
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim dDiferencaEnt As Double
    Dim dDiferencaSai As Double
    Dim dIntroduzidoEnt As Double
    Dim dIntroduzidoSai As Double

    On Error GoTo erro

    If Index > 0 Then
        oValidate.OnLostFocus txtCxDiaria(Index), vtDouble
        
        'correcção de caixa relativa a PAT 7449 por EC FMD
        If Config_CaixaIntroducaoSaidaNC Then
            lblCxValores(Index + 10).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(Index).Text) - Abs(IIf(lblCxValores(Index).Caption > 0, lblCxValores(Index).Caption, 0)), "Standard")
        Else
            lblCxValores(Index + 10).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(Index).Text) - Abs(lblCxValores(Index).Caption), "Standard")
        End If
        If Index = 1 Then
            lblCxValores(11).Caption = Format$(oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(11).Caption) + m_CaixaFM, "Standard")
        End If
        
        
        'lblCxValores(20).Caption = (lblCxValores(11).Caption + lblCxValores(12).Caption + lblCxValores(13).Caption + lblCxValores(14).Caption + lblCxValores(15).Caption + lblCxValores(16).Caption) - (lblCxValores(17).Caption + lblCxValores(18).Caption + lblCxValores(19).Caption)

        dDiferencaEnt = oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(11).Caption) + _
                        oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(12).Caption) + _
                        oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(13).Caption) + _
                        oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(14).Caption) + _
                        oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(15).Caption) + _
                        oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(16).Caption) + _
                        m_CaixaFM
                        
        dDiferencaSai = oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(17).Caption) + _
                        oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(18).Caption) + _
                        oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(19).Caption)

        lblCxValores(20).Caption = Format$(dDiferencaEnt - dDiferencaSai, "Standard")

        dIntroduzidoEnt = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(1).Text) + _
                          oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(2).Text) + _
                          oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(3).Text) + _
                          oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(4).Text) + _
                          oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(5).Text) + _
                          oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(6).Text)
                          
        If Config_GetRemoverNotasCreditoTotalCaixa Then
            dIntroduzidoEnt = dIntroduzidoEnt - oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(6).Text)
        End If
                          
                          
        'correcção de caixa relativa a PAT 7449 por EC FMD
        If Config_Caixa_SubtraiDevolucoes Then
            dIntroduzidoSai = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(9).Text)
        Else
            dIntroduzidoSai = 0
        End If
        'correcção de caixa relativa a PAT 7449 por EC FMD

        lblCxValores(21).Caption = Format$(dIntroduzidoEnt - Abs(dIntroduzidoSai), "Standard")
        'lblCxValores(20).Caption = Format$(Abs(lblCxValores(21).Caption) - Abs(lblCxValores(21).Caption), "Standard")
        
        If Index <> 10 Then
            If dDiferencaEnt + dDiferencaSai > 0 And (dDiferencaEnt - m_CaixaFM) >= 0 Then
                txtCxDiaria(10).Text = Format$(dDiferencaEnt + dDiferencaSai, "Standard")
                lblCxValores(20).Caption = Format$(0, "Standard")
            Else
                txtCxDiaria(10).Text = Format$(0, "Standard")
                lblCxValores(20).Caption = Format$(dDiferencaEnt - m_CaixaFM, "Standard")
            End If
        End If
        
      
        
        '        lDummy = oUtils.FormatNumber(txtCxDiaria(Index).Text, 2, 3, sDecSeparador, sMilSeparador, sAux)
        '        txtCxDiaria(Index).Text = sAux
        '
        '        If Index <> 10 Then
        '            xlbl = oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(Index + 10).Tag)
        '            xtxt = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtCxDiaria(Index).Text)
        '
        '            'xlbl = xlbl + xtxt
        '            xlbl = xtxt - xlbl
        '            lDummy = oUtils.FormatNumber(xlbl, 2, 3, sDecSeparador, sMilSeparador, sAux)
        '            lblCxValores(Index + 10).Caption = sAux
        '            For Each xObjTxt In txtCxDiaria
        '                xtxtTotal = xtxtTotal + oUtils.Convert2Double(xObjTxt.Text)
        '            Next
        '            xlblTotal = oUtils.Convert2Double(lblCxValores(20).Tag)
        '            lDummy = oUtils.FormatNumber(xtxtTotal, 2, 3, sDecSeparador, sMilSeparador, sAux)
        '            lblCxValores(21).Caption = sAux
        '            lDummy = oUtils.FormatNumber(xtxtTotal + xlblTotal, 2, 3, sDecSeparador, sMilSeparador, sAux)
        '            lblCxValores(20).Caption = sAux
        '
        '        End If
        '
    Else
        oValidate.OnLostFocus txtCxDiaria(Index), vtNone
    End If
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "txtCxDiaria_LostFocus()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose

End Sub


Private Sub txtDoc_Change(Index As Integer)
    Dim sText1 As String


    sText1 = Trim$(txtDoc(0).Text)
    If Not txtDoc(1).Visible Then
        With chkDoc(1)
            If sText1 <> "" And cboDoc(2).ListIndex <> 7 Then
                .Enabled = True
            Else
                .Enabled = False
                .value = 0
            End If
        End With
    End If
End Sub

    oValidate.OnGotFocus txtDoc(Index)
End Sub

    End Select

End Sub

    End Select
End Sub

'
Private Sub txtIntroducao_GotFocus(Index As Integer)

'txtIntroducao(Index).Text = vbNullString

End Sub

Private Sub txtIntroducao_KeyDown(Index As Integer, KeyCode As Integer, Shift As Integer)
    Dim iColuna As Integer, iSelStart As Integer
    Dim iErro As Integer
    On Error GoTo erro

    iSelStart = txtIntroducao(Index).SelStart
    iColuna = tdgVenda.Col

    Select Case KeyCode
        Case vbKeyUp
            If tdgVenda.Row <> 0 Then
                If IsNull(tdgVenda.bookmark) Then
                    tdgVenda.MoveLast
                Else
                    tdgVenda.MovePrevious
                End If
                tdgVenda.SetFocus
            End If

        Case vbKeyDown
            If xaVendas.UpperBound(1) <> tdgVenda.Row Then
                If IsNull(tdgVenda.bookmark) Then
                    tdgVenda.MoveLast
                Else
                    tdgVenda.MoveNext
                End If
                tdgVenda.SetFocus
            End If

        Case vbKeyLeft
            If iSelStart = 0 Then
                Select Case Index
                    Case 1    ' Descricao
                        iColuna = VendaCol_Referencia

                    Case 2    ' Qt
                        iColuna = VendaCol_Descricao

                    Case 3    ' Iva
                        iColuna = VendaCol_Qt

                    Case 4    ' Preco
                        iColuna = VendaCol_Iva

                    Case 5    ' desconto
                        iColuna = VendaCol_Preco

                End Select
                tdgVenda.SetFocus

            End If

        Case vbKeyRight
            If iSelStart = Len(txtIntroducao(Index).Text) Then
                Select Case Index
                    Case 0    ' Referencia
                        iColuna = VendaCol_Descricao

                    Case 1    ' Descricao
                        iColuna = VendaCol_Qt

                    Case 2    ' Qt
                        iColuna = VendaCol_Iva

                    Case 3    ' Iva
                        iColuna = VendaCol_Preco

                    Case 4    ' Preco
                        iColuna = VendaCol_Desconto

                    Case 5    ' desconto
                        iColuna = VendaCol_Referencia

                End Select
                tdgVenda.SetFocus

            End If

    End Select
    tdgVenda.Col = iColuna

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "txtIntroducao_KeyDown()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub txtIntroducao_KeyPress(Index As Integer, KeyAscii As Integer)

    Dim iDec As Integer, iUnid As Integer, iPos As Integer
    Dim iColuna As Integer
    Dim iErro As Integer

    On Error GoTo erro

    Select Case KeyAscii
        Case vbKeyEscape
            txtIntroducao(Index).Text = tdgVenda.Text
            tdgVenda.SetFocus

        Case vbKeyReturn
            tdgVenda.SetFocus
            If Index < 5 Then iColuna = Index + 1: tdgVenda.Col = iColuna

            '    Case vbKeyUp
            '        If tdgVenda.Row <> 0 Then
            '            tdgVenda.SetFocus
            '            tdgVenda.MovePrevious
            '        End If
            '
            '    Case vbKeyDown
            '        If xaVendas.UpperBound(1) <> tdgVenda.Row Then
            '            tdgVenda.SetFocus
            '            tdgVenda.MoveNext
            '        End If

        Case Else
            Select Case Index
                Case 2, 4, 5
                    iDec = GetSystemDecimalPlaces(): iUnid = 3
                    If Index > 2 Then
                        iDec = 2
                        iUnid = IIf(tdgVenda.Columns(Index).Caption = "Desc. %", 3, 6)
                    End If
                    With txtIntroducao(Index)
                        iPos = .SelStart
                        oValidate.ValidNumber .Text, sDecSeparador, KeyAscii, iPos, iUnid, iDec
                    End With
            End Select
    End Select

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "txtIntroducao_KeyPress()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub txtIntroducao_LostFocus(Index As Integer)

    Dim sCheckDigit As String
    Dim iErro As Integer

    On Error GoTo erro

    If Index = 0 Then
        If Len(txtIntroducao(0).Text) = 13 Then
            If IsNumeric(txtIntroducao(0).Text) Then
                sCheckDigit = txtIntroducao(0).Text
                sCheckDigit = oUtils.CheckDigit(sCheckDigit)
                txtIntroducao(0).Text = Mid(txtIntroducao(0).Text, 1, 12) & sCheckDigit
            End If
        End If
    End If

    If (Index = 5) And (tdgVenda.Columns(Index).Caption = "Desc. %") Then
        If (val(txtIntroducao(5).Text & vbNullString) > 100) Then
            Beep
            txtIntroducao(5).Text = "0"
        End If
    End If

    If CarregaGridVendas(Index) Then Exit Sub
    Select Case Index
        Case 2, 4, 5
            Cal_QtPreco
    End Select

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "txtIntroducao_LostFocus()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub txtVenda_Change(Index As Integer)

    Dim dvEntregue As Double
    Dim dvRecebe As Double
    Dim dvPagar As Double
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim dTotal As Double
    Dim dTroco As Double

    On Error GoTo erro


    Select Case Index


        Case 14    '  Nota de credito


        Case 7, 12, 13, 15    'Valor a receber

            dTotal = edValores.Total
            lblValorEntregue.Caption = Format$(dTotal, "standard")
            If dTotal >= oUtils.Convert2Double(lblTotais(1).Caption) Then
                ibnReceber.value = oUtils.Convert2Double(lblTotais(1).Caption)
            Else
                ibnReceber.value = dTotal
            End If
            dTroco = dTotal - ibnReceber.value
            If dTroco <= 0 Then
                dTroco = 0
            End If
            lblTroco.Caption = Format$(dTroco, "standard")

    End Select
    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "txtVenda_Change()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub txtVenda_GotFocus(Index As Integer)
    Dim iErro As Integer
    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim lDummy As Boolean
    Dim dValorAux As Double

    Select Case Index
        Case 7, 12, 13
            dValorAux = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtVenda(Index).Text)
            txtVenda(Index).Text = oUtils.Convert2Double(txtVenda(Index).Text)
            If dValorAux > 0 Then txtVenda(Index).Text = dValorAux
            oValidate.OnGotFocus txtVenda(Index), vbRightJustify, True

        Case Else
            oValidate.OnGotFocus txtVenda(Index)

    End Select

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "txtVenda_GotFocus()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub


Private Sub txtVenda_KeyPress(Index As Integer, KeyAscii As Integer)

    Dim iPos As Integer
    Dim iErro As Integer

    On Error GoTo erro

    Select Case Index
        Case 1
            If KeyAscii = 13 Then tdgVenda.SetFocus

        Case 7, 13, 12
            oValidate.OnKeyPress txtVenda(Index), KeyAscii, vtDouble
            With txtVenda(Index)
                iPos = .SelStart
                oValidate.ValidNumber .Text, sDecSeparador, KeyAscii, iPos, 9, 2
                If .SelStart <> iPos Then .SelStart = iPos
            End With
        Case 14
            oValidate.OnKeyPress txtVenda(Index), KeyAscii, vtNone
        Case Else
            oValidate.OnKeyPress txtVenda(Index), KeyAscii, vtNone

    End Select

    If (KeyAscii = vbKeyReturn) Then KeyAscii = 0

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "txtVenda_KeyPress()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub

Private Sub txtVenda_LostFocus(Index As Integer)
    On Error GoTo erro
    Dim iErro As Integer
    Dim sCodigo1 As String
    Dim sCodigo2 As String
    Dim sLocalidade As String
    Dim iResult As Integer
    
    Select Case Index
        Case 1
            Dim cliNumero As Double, cliNumeroAnterior As Long
            cliNumero = val(txtVenda(1).Text)
            If cliNumero > 2147483647 Then
                MsgBox "O cliente com número " & cliNumero & " não existe.", vbExclamation
                Exit Sub
            End If
            
            If cliNumero = 0 Then
                txtVenda(1).Text = ""
                Exit Sub
            End If
                                    
            With datClientes.Recordset
                If .EOF Then
                    MsgBox "Ainda não foi criada nenhuma ficha de cliente.", vbExclamation, "Cliente"
                    txtVenda(1).Text = ""
                    Exit Sub
                End If
                
                cliNumeroAnterior = !cliNumero
                .FindFirst "clinumero = " & cliNumero
                    
                If Not .NoMatch Then
                    lIdCliente = !cliID

                    dbcVenda(2).Text = IfNull(!CliNome, "")
                    txtVenda(2).Text = IfNull(!cliMorada, "")
                    
                    DivideCodigoPostal !cpCodigo, sCodigo1, sCodigo2
                    txtVenda(3).Text = sCodigo1
                    txtVenda(9).Text = sCodigo2
                    
                    txtVenda(4).Text = IfNull(!cpLocalidade, "")
                    txtVenda(5).Text = IfNull(!cliTelCasa, "")
                    txtVenda(6).Text = IfNull(!cliLocalidade, "")
                Else
                    MsgBox "O cliente com número " & cliNumero & " não existe.", vbExclamation
                    txtVenda(1).Text = cliNumeroAnterior
                End If
            End With

        Case 3, 9    'Cod. Postal

            If (Me.ActiveControl.Name = "cmdVenda") Then
                If (Me.ActiveControl.Index = 1) Then
                    Exit Sub
                End If
            End If

            iResult = CarregarCodigoPostal(txtVenda(3).Text, txtVenda(9).Text, sLocalidade)
            If (iResult <> RES_SUCCESS) Then GoTo Abortar
            txtVenda(4).Text = sLocalidade
    End Select

    oValidate.OnLostFocus txtVenda(Index), vtNone

    Exit Sub
erro:
    iErro = ErrorHandle("frmPosMain", "txtVenda_LostFocus()")
    Select Case iErro
        Case ERRO_UNKNOWN: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME: Resume 0
        Case ERRO_RESUME_NEXT: Resume Next
        Case ERRO_RESUME_ABORT: Resume Abortar
        Case ERRO_RESUME_END: Sair
    End Select
Abortar:       On Error Resume Next
    bSemaforo bClose
End Sub
